1935.10.07

A-Army Fights Bravely for Three Days and Nights: A-Duwa Falls, a Decisive Victory. Italian Army Concentrates Large Forces for Continued Advance; A-Country Strengthens Eastern Line of Defense.

A-Jing: After three days and nights of siege by the Italian army, A-Duwa city is said to have fallen (Havas dispatch, 6th).

A-Si-Ma-La: A dispatch from the Italian front reports that the Italian army has captured A-Duwa town (Reuters dispatch, 6th).

A-Si-Ma-La: After extremely fierce fighting near A-Duwa in the past forty-eight hours, the Italian army has today captured the ancient city of A-Duwa (Reuters dispatch, 6th).

(Rome) While the Italian army's war report from A-Si-Ma-La, Eritrea, claims that A-Duwa has already fallen, the official Roman bulletin on the progress of the Abyssinian war does not mention this. According to the bulletin, the first legion commanded by General Santini has raised the Italian flag at the ruins of the old fort of A-Di-La-Te, north of A-Duwa. Residents and clergy have surrendered. The second legion has reached the edge of the A-Duwa valley and continues to advance this morning. The Italian army in the southeast has occupied Jie-Luo-Gu-Bi town after a brief battle (Reuters dispatch, 6th).

A-Jing: According to news received here, the Italian army concentrated a large part of its forces to besiege A-Duwa city for three days and nights, but the city has not yet fallen. Last night, the Italian and A-armies engaged in close combat in the Tang-Na-Kai area southeast of A-Duwa city, with hundreds of Italian soldiers killed. 15,000 A-country regular troops have rushed from the capital to the vicinity of A-Duwa to reinforce General Sai-Xiong, the governor of Tigre province, who is defending the area. However, it is feared that it may be too late, and A-She-Hua city will ultimately be indefensible. It is rumored that the A-army has infiltrated Italian-controlled Eritrea, cutting off the Italian army's rear transportation. Furthermore, the Italian army on the southern front is advancing on the Wo-Jia-Deng area from Italian Somaliland. The A-army stationed in Ha-La-Er has now been fully deployed to the nearby border area of Qi-Qi-Jia (Jijiga) to block them (Havas dispatch, 5th).

(Rome) Italian newspapers report frontline news stating that the A-army is currently using guerrilla tactics to impede the Italian army's advance north of A-Duwa. The Italian army is now changing tactics, planning to gather tanks and aircraft to attack A-Duwa from the rear along the A-Duwa to A-Ji-Mu (Akim) road. Although the Italian army encountered fierce resistance in Mei-Ba-Li-Ya (Maibaria), they have occupied several small mountains, from which they are shelling A-Duwa, ten miles away.

A-Jing: Ten thousand A-army soldiers have been ordered to defend Mount Mu-Sa-A-Li in the northeastern corner of A-country at all costs, because the A-king has declared that if the area falls, the railway between Djibouti and A-Jing will be cut off. Italian aircraft bombed the towns of A-Duwa and A-Di-Ge-La, causing little bloodshed, because the residents of the towns had all fled to the surrounding countryside before the war began. At 4 PM today, the authorities issued a statement stating that Italian troops had occupied our outposts in Hua-Qi-La (Wagela) and An-Ju-La (Enguela), suffering heavy casualties. Italian troops have advanced to within a few miles of A-Di-Ge-La, which is still being defended by our troops (Reuters dispatch, 5th).

A-Jing: The A-government tonight admitted that the Italian army is advancing gradually along three routes: east, south, and north. However, the main battle has not yet begun. The A-army's purpose in defending the border is not to stop the Italian advance, but rather to intercept them in various sections. Rumors that the A-army suffered 1,500 casualties in the battle of A-Duwa have been denied here. The A-emperor is now awaiting Italian air strikes on the capital, as the Italian army on the eastern and southern fronts are both advancing towards the railway line. After they converge, it is quite possible that they will immediately build an air force base (National Telegram, 5th).

Rome Announces War Report: Northern Army Advances One Hundred Miles; Mussolini's Son-in-Law Narrowly Escapes Disaster

(Rome) An official bulletin was issued here this afternoon, for the first time officially acknowledging that the Italian army has invaded Abyssinia from Somaliland. It states that the Italian army has occupied Dolo, near the northeastern border of Kenya. Italian aircraft bombed Gorahai, about 100 miles northwest, located within Abyssinian territory. At the same time, according to the "Jiang Tan Bao", the A-government has begun to inspect wireless telegrams sent from A-Jing. It also states that a large batch of British-made munitions is being transported from the port of Jira in British Somaliland into A-country to supply the garrison of Ha-La-Er (Reuters dispatch, 5th).

(Rome) A frontline war report received here today states that Count Ciano, Mussolini's son-in-law (formerly the Italian ambassador to China), narrowly escaped disaster. While flying over A-territory in his plane, it was struck by several bullets and damaged. However, the Count escaped injury and safely flew back to Asmara in Italian Somaliland. It is noted that Count Ciano commanded the air force that launched a fierce attack on A-Duwa when the Italian army launched its offensive against A on October 3rd (Reuters dispatch, 5th).

The Mighty Italian Army Launches Three-Pronged Attack: A-Army Employs Strategy of Luring the Enemy Deep; Fighting Bravely with Four Against Ten

A-Jing: This area recently received a report from General Sai-Xiong, the governor of Tigre province, stating that the Italian army occupied the two defense camps of Wa-Jie-Da (Waheta) and An-Ge-La (Enguela) at 4 PM yesterday (south of A-Duwa city). Both sides suffered heavy casualties. Four Italian officers were killed on the spot. Our army also captured two machine guns and two rifles. Italian aircraft carried out bombings near the city of A-Di-Ge-La, killing many women and children. The regiment has now advanced to Bietharpariat (about one and a half hours walk from the city of A-Di-Ge-La). The country's planes fly back and forth over the place. As for the claim that an Italian plane was shot down by the A-army yesterday, the A-government has not verified it. According to a communiqué issued here, the Italian army on the northern route has advanced 100 kilometers, aiming to encircle the cities of A-Duwa, A-Ke-Sen (Aksum), and Bing, and capture them in one fell swoop. As for the A-army, its main force has not yet joined the war. The strategy adopted is to avoid direct conflict with the Italian army and lure the enemy deep into a suitable location, before launching a counter-offensive. The famous A-general, General Jia-Sa, originally led a large force stationed in the mountainous area around Gong-Da-Er city (southwest of A-Duwa city) and is now preparing to rush to A-Duwa city to support General Sai-Xiong. The Italian army is currently launching attacks along three routes: one is the northern route, starting north of the Da-Bu-Si River (Takkaxe) in Tigre province, heading directly for A-Duwa city; one is the middle route, advancing eastward towards Wo-Sa-You (Aussa), Ha-Tai-Er-Ju-Bo city (Hadelegubo, close to French Somaliland); and one is the southern route, starting from Italian Somaliland, now advancing southeast towards the Wo-Jia-Deng (Ogaden) area and Jie-Luo-Gu-Bi city. At present, the Italian armies on all routes have only made contact with the A-army's outposts, and the main battle has not yet occurred. As for the Italian aircraft bombing A-Duwa city, the number of casualties included 40 women and 32 children. When the Italian and A-armies fought in the cities of A-Duwa and A-Ke-Sen, the A-army's strength was only 400 men, yet they were able to resist 1,000 Italian soldiers. It is reported that 45 A-soldiers were killed, while 21 Italian soldiers were killed, and 65 were captured. In addition, the Italian troops concentrated on Mount Mu-Sa-Li-Ya (that is, the place where the Italian army first invaded A-territory) numbered 30,000 men, with 70 tanks and 100 aircraft (Havas dispatch, 5th).

Northern Front War Situation

A-Duwa Under Encirclement - A-Si-Ma-La City

Our special correspondent declares that the three columns of Italian troops starting from Eritrea reached their destination yesterday. (1) The Sandini column has occupied the city of A-Di-Ge-La in A-country. (2) The Bier-Qi-Wo-Ci-Luo-Li column has occupied An-De-Suo-Yi-Wo (Entisoiu). (3) The Ma-La-Wei-Ge-Na column has arrived near A-Duwa city and is expected to occupy the city in a few hours. The Italian army has not yet encountered strong resistance. As for the A-Jing's report that an Italian plane was shot down, officials here have denied it (Havas dispatch, 6th).

Nine Columns Advance - A-Si-Ma-La

Our visiting reporter declares that Italian aircraft on the northern route reconnoitered this morning and discovered two large columns of A-army troops advancing towards the front line, about ten kilometers from the Italian army. As for the Italian consul in A-Duwa city, Fu-Lang-Jia, who had previously received instructions to leave his post, before the consul could comply, he was arrested by the A-authorities. The headquarters here have not received any news about his whereabouts. At present, nine columns of Italian troops are advancing on different routes. The division commanded by General Ma-La-Wei-Ge-Na is on the right wing, with colonial native troops in the center, and the Italian army headquarters troops commanded by General Sandini on the left wing, guided by native troops, in order to harmonize with the people along the way. In short, the large Italian army is concentrating between the cities of A-Di-Ge-La and A-Duwa, carrying tanks to assist in the battle, and with engineers accompanying them to immediately build roads after the main army advances, in order to facilitate rear transportation. The air force is serving as liaison between the various columns. The area through which the Italian army's right wing passes is mostly hilly, with many civilian houses on the hills. The A-army is hiding in them, fiercely resisting, and thus fierce fighting has broken out between the two sides. However, the right-wing commander, General Ma-La-Wei-Ge-Na, still defeated the A-soldiers and advanced to the vicinity of A-Duwa city (Havas dispatch, 5th).

A-Jing: The government has just declared that the Italian air force bombed Sai-Ke-Tai city, which is 160 kilometers south of A-Duwa city, has a population of 15,000, and is an important city. The government has just approved the dispatch of 150 French colonial army personnel to Di-Lai-Da-Hua city (Diredawa) along the railway (north of Ha-La-Er city) to protect railway staff (Havas dispatch, 6th).

30,000 Italian Troops Continue to Reinforce (Rome) It is reported that approximately 35,000 Italian troops are currently en route in the Red Sea, intending to go to Italian Eritrea. The port facilities at Masua are now being greatly improved, with the capacity to disembark 3,000 soldiers and 3,000 tons of munitions daily (Havas dispatch, 5th).

Disseminated Leaflets Advise Indigenous People (Rome) It is reported that Italian aircraft are distributing leaflets in northern A-country, advising the indigenous people to surrender to Italy, saying that the Italian army is extremely powerful and will mercilessly punish anyone who dares to resist. It also said, "Before the A-emperor destroyed the territory of Emperor Xu-An of Tigre, Italy should now restore the Xu-An dynasty to its original position. The A-government is making a big mistake by forbidding you from selling goods to Eritrea. If the Amhara people (the central ethnic group of A-country) invade Tigre province, they will plunder your livestock and goods. Only the Italians can benefit you, because the Italians are loved by God," (Havas dispatch, 5th).

Eastern Front War Situation

Tai-Xi City Suffers Tragic Bombing - A-Jing: It is rumored that Italian aircraft bombed Dessie city, 250 kilometers north of the capital, but the details are unknown. The A-army declares that it captured 40 Italian soldiers in the Tang-Na-Kai area on the northern border. Also, trains departing from the capital are fully loaded with military supplies destined for Ha-La-Er. The governor of Arussi province, Ma-Li-An, arrived here tonight to receive instructions from the A-emperor. The governor of Wallega province in western A-country, Mai-Ge-Nan, will soon pass through the capital leading troops to the north to fight (Havas dispatch, 5th).

Southern Front War Situation

Hua-Er-Hua-Er Announces Recapture - A-Jing: A visiting reporter received news from the southern front that the A-army in the Wo-Jia-Deng area had besieged Hua-Er-Hua-Er and recaptured the place. It is noted that Hua-Er-Hua-Er has been occupied by Italy since December of last year. This Italian-A conflict also started with this as the starting point (Haswa dispatch, 6th).

Italian Nationals Overseas Return to Country to Enlist in Military

(Rome) Italian citizens residing in Thessaloniki and Piraeus, Greece, have returned to their country to join the army. They have recently arrived in Brindisi and were warmly welcomed by local government officials and people. In addition, hundreds of volunteer soldiers from Italian communities in Argentina, Brazil, and Uruguay in South America are now on their way back to the country. All volunteer soldiers returning from abroad are currently undergoing centralized training in the city of Sabadia, numbering 4,000. They have formed an overseas community corps, commanded by Balini, the chairman of the Overseas Chinese Association. The training will be completed within two months. It is noted that Sapodia is a newly built city under the Fascist regime (Havas, 6th).

Geneva Takes a Sharp Turn: Which is the Aggressor Nation Needs to be Determined Urgently; League of Nations Forms Six-Person Committee to Research; Voices for Sanctions Against Italy

(Geneva) At an important meeting of the League of Nations Administrative Council today, A representative Ha-Hua-Li-Te formally stated that he was seeking to adopt the sanctions stipulated in Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant against Italy. The Administrative Council considered the report of the Thirteen-Person Committee, but has not yet passed it, because the representatives of both Italy and A have just received the original text of the report and need to seek instructions from their home governments. The Administrative Council designated the representatives of England, France, Spain, Romania, Portugal, and Chile to form a Six-Person Committee to study the situation based on the reports of the disputing countries and to determine which is the aggressor nation. It is expected that the Six-Person Committee will be able to decide on this point on Sunday. After the aggressor nation is determined, the League of Nations can take the second step, which is to consider sanctions. People in Geneva generally believe that the current situation will inevitably move towards the adoption of sanctions, which is truly an unprecedented event in the history of the League of Nations.

The League of Nations General Assembly is scheduled to meet at 4 PM on Wednesday, at which time the first step regarding sanctions may be taken. The British representative Eden advocated that the newly organized Six-Person Committee should immediately start work. This proposal has now been realized, which shows that the Administrative Council has decided not to delay any longer. The Six-Person Committee met for an hour tonight and elected the Portuguese representative Monteiro as chairman, and decided to meet again tomorrow afternoon. At the same time, it instructed the Secretariat to prepare a complete file of all documents regarding the case (Reuters dispatch, 5th).

(Geneva) The League of Nations began today to confirm Italy as the instigator of the war against A-country, which is a prelude to the implementation of sanctions. The League of Nations Administrative Council tonight separately nominated the six countries of England, France, Russia, Portugal, Denmark, and Chile to form a drafting committee to produce another report, which is to be submitted to the Administrative Council for formal discussion on Monday. The League of Nations General Assembly has also decided to meet on Wednesday. Geneva is experiencing a sharp turn of events (National Telegram, 5th).

(Geneva) Whether or not sanctions will be implemented is no longer a question. However, what kind of sanctions should be adopted remains to be decided. The report of the Six-Person Committee designated by the League of Nations Administrative Council yesterday to study the new situation and determine which is the aggressor nation will inevitably lead to a ruling that Italy has violated Articles 10, 12, and 15 of the League of Nations Covenant. This is undoubtedly certain. It is expected that this report will be unanimously passed by the Administrative Council, and then it will be transferred to the League of Nations General Assembly, which will convene at 4 PM on Wednesday to establish a committee to decide what kind of sanctions can be implemented in the current situation (Reuters dispatch, 6th).

Administrative Council Meeting Held the Day Before Yesterday: Atmosphere Extremely Tense; Eleven Committees Submit Reports; League of Nations General Assembly Convened on Wednesday

(Geneva) When the Administrative Council met at 6 PM tonight to accept the report of the Thirteen-Person Committee, the meeting hall was crowded and the atmosphere was extremely tense. The severity of the situation could be seen on everyone's faces. The Italian representative Aroccios and the A representative Ha-Hua-Li-Te sat facing each other at the horseshoe-shaped table (Reuters dispatch, 5th).

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council met this afternoon, first holding a closed-door meeting attended by the representatives of thirteen countries, including England, France, the Soviet Union, Romania, Argentina, Equatorial Guinea, Chile, Spain, Australia, Poland, and Denmark. The Italian representative Aroccios and the Abyssinian representative Ha-Hua-Li-Te waited in the adjacent room in the meeting hall. At 6 PM, a public meeting was held, and the Italian and A representatives attended the meeting.

Italian Representative Vigorously Defends Himself

First, the Italian representative Aroccios read a lengthy speech, stating briefly that the Italian government regretted that the League of Nations Administrative Council was unwilling to examine the situation from a practical point of view. The Italian government believed that if it did not understand the actual situation in Abyssinia after years of continuous harassment of Italy by the A-country, and only made a superficial judgment, it would inevitably misidentify the aggressor as the aggressed. As for the hostility of some foreign public opinion towards Italy, it was for other reasons and had nothing to do with the Italian-A conflict. This Italian military action was a response to the A-country's mobilization (Havas dispatch, 5th). Finally, he said that the Italian government deeply appreciated the efforts of the Administrative Council, but the League of Nations had already understood and hoped that the first thing to be considered was that Abyssinia was not qualified to join the League of Nations (Reuters dispatch, 5th).

A Representative Requests Sanctions

Next, the A representative Ha-Hua-Li-Te read the note from the Abyssinian government to the League of Nations, which was issued this afternoon (see separate telegram), and said that although the A-country had been repeatedly subjected to Italian military threats, the A-country's mobilization order was delayed until the last minute before it was issued. The A-country now requested that the League of Nations Administrative Council take the procedures described in Article 16 of the Covenant and immediately order the Italian government to cease military action. Thereupon, the chairman of the Administrative Council, the Argentine representative Qi-Na-Ge, declared that the Administrative Council would continue to meet next Sunday to vote on the Administrative Council's report on the Italian-A dispute. The Administrative Council adjourned at 6:45 PM. It was also heard that at today's closed-door meeting of the Administrative Council, based on the recommendation of the Thirteen-Nation Committee, it was decided to convene the League of Nations General Assembly next Wednesday to order a determination of who was at fault. After the League of Nations determined the aggressor country, a drafting committee would be established to draft a sanctions plan. Also, at today's meeting of the Administrative Council, the representatives of the six countries of England, France, the Soviet Union, Portugal, Chile, and Denmark were entrusted to prepare the report of the Administrative Council based on the report prepared by the Thirteen-Nation Committee (see separate telegram) and submit it for voting at the meeting next Sunday (Havas dispatch, 5th).

Report of the Thirteen-Nation Committee: The Internal Situation in A-country is Now Different From Before; Proving the Inappropriateness of Italian Actions

(Geneva) The Thirteen-Nation Committee today submitted a report to the League of Nations Administrative Council on the origin and course of the Italian-A dispute. The report described in detail the past and present situation of the relations between Italy and A-country. It was particularly interesting to analyze the memorandum submitted by Italy to the League of Nations on September 4th and the A-country's reply. It briefly stated that Italy's memorandum expressed dissatisfaction with the A-country in three points: (1) The Italian border in East Africa was not secure; (2) The A-country did not fulfill the obligations it assumed when it joined the League of Nations; and (3) Internal disturbances in A-country were not stable. Subsequently, the A-country government sent a note to the League of Nations on September 14, proposing that the League of Nations send a survey team to the local area to investigate the points that Italy considered unsatisfactory. However, the Thirteen-Nation Committee regretted that it was unable to send a survey team to the area in the current situation. As for the Italian memorandum's claim that the Italian border was not secure, the report pointed out that the East African territories of England and France, which were connected to the border of the A-country, were also frequently violated and incidents occurred. However, England and France always sought to resolve the matter through diplomatic channels. The Thirteen-Nation Committee believed that even if there were border violations, they were not of an aggressive nature and were all the actions of local tribes. The A-country central government never encouraged them. Regarding the second point in the Italian memorandum, the report acknowledged that although the A-emperor had used all possible means to prohibit the slave system, there was actually little progress. Regarding the third point in the Italian memorandum, the report stated that when the A-country joined the League of Nations in 1923, the internal disturbances in the A-country were known to the countries that guaranteed the A-country's accession to the League of Nations at that time. The current internal situation in the A-country is no worse than in 1923. On the contrary, on the surface, the internal situation in the A-country is indeed more unified and stronger than before. The A-country needs foreign cooperation and assistance to improve its internal situation. The A-country representative admitted this point in his speech to the League of Nations General Assembly on September 11th of this year. In short, regarding the problems of the A-country, unless they are based on respect for the independence, integrity, and security of the member states of the League of Nations, there is no other way to solve them. Also, the Italian memorandum was delivered to the League of Nations on September 4th of this year, but the A-country first submitted its application to the League of Nations on December 14th of last year. After the A-country submitted its application, the Italian government opposed the League of Nations Administrative Council's discussion of the Italian-A issue and continued to send troops to East Africa. Since the beginning of the Italian-A dispute, the Abyssinian government has consistently sought a peaceful solution. The A-country has accepted and requested that neutral observers be sent to the local area for investigation. On the contrary, after the arbitration and resolution of the Hua-Er-Hua-Er conflict, Italy still demanded free action against the A-country and repeatedly stated that the situation in the A-country was special and could not be resolved by applying the League of Nations Covenant (Havas dispatch, 5th).

Page 4

Two Proposals

From the above suggestions of the Thirteen Committee's report, if Italy stops the war and withdraws its troops in the A-country, negotiations can now be conducted based on Article 15 of the Covenant, which stipulates that the administrative organ should peacefully resolve disputes. If Article 12 of the Covenant is, as expected, found to be actually violated, then sanctions should be adopted, and a committee to handle the adoption of sanctions will be established.

Sanction Steps

The first step of sanctions will be economic and financial in nature, and the severance of diplomatic relations between member states and the aggressor country is also within this plan. The second step will be the cancellation of the ban on the supply of munitions to the aggressed country and the ban on all supplies to the aggressor country (Reuters dispatch, 5th).

The Abyssinian Government Sends a Note to the League of Nations, Requesting Sanctions Against Italy, Invoking Article 16, Section 2 of the Covenant, Vowing to Resist to the End to Defend National Territory

(Geneva) The Abyssinian government recently delivered another note to the Secretariat of the League of Nations, stating, "The Abyssinian government respectfully and resolutely applies to the Council of the League of Nations, requesting that, based on the facts reported in the Emperor's previous telegram, it officially declare that, according to the interpretation of Article 16 of the Covenant of the League of Nations, Italy has engaged in war. Therefore, the consequences stipulated in Article 16, Section 1 of the Covenant (i.e., a country engaged in aggression should be regarded as having committed an act of war against all members of the League of Nations, and other members should impose economic and financial sanctions) should, in fact, be deemed to have been established. The Abyssinian government further requests the Council to fulfill the obligations stipulated in Article 16, Section 2 of the Covenant (i.e., the Council should recommend to the governments of the countries concerned to take effective military measures to maintain the effectiveness of the Covenant), so that the armed conflict that violates the law and sacred covenants will be quickly terminated. The Abyssinian government hereby declares that the people of Abyssinia are prepared to shed their last drop of blood to defend Abyssinian independence and territorial integrity, resolutely and unyieldingly resisting this unjust war. Even if the enemy troops possess superior weapons and are cruelly and insatiably slaughtering, the Abyssinian people will never submit to violence, for the Abyssinian people deeply know that they are sacrificing not only to defend Abyssinia but also for the independence of all small and weak countries. If an aggressor who uses violence is allowed to achieve victory without resistance, then all small and weak countries in the world will become prey. For this reason, the Abyssinian government hereby applies again to the League of Nations, reiterating that treaties must be respected, that war is illegal, and that it is awaiting orders with utmost urgency." (Havas dispatch, 5th)

The United States Implements an Arms Embargo, Facilitating League of Nations Sanctions, Welcomed by London and Geneva

(Washington) President Roosevelt issued a proclamation today, stating that a state of war exists between Italy and Abyssinia. Therefore, the measures stipulated in the U.S. Neutrality Act, prohibiting the transportation of arms to belligerent countries, will naturally be effectively implemented. This embargo is limited to arms but does not include raw materials. What is prohibited includes various rifles and machine guns, various ammunition, various warships, various aircraft (whether military or civilian, whole or in parts), aircraft engines, mustard gas, and flamethrowers, etc. According to recent statistics released by the State Department, the United States has rarely transported arms to Abyssinia. Therefore, Abyssinia will not be affected by this embargo, but Italy will lose its source of aircraft parts and engines. As for other arms, exports to Italy are of little importance. President Roosevelt is still aboard the cruiser Houston. After receiving the State Department's official report on the war between Italy and Abyssinia, he decided to issue the aforementioned proclamation and sent a wireless message to Secretary of State Hull, instructing him to handle the matter accordingly. President Roosevelt also issued the following remarks: "Although we have held out hope that war could be avoided, and we have made efforts in this regard, we can only acknowledge the simple and certain fact that Italian and Abyssinian troops are now engaged in combat, and the state of war referred to in the Neutrality Act now exists. Under these special circumstances, I want to make it clear to the people that anyone who voluntarily engages in any form of transaction with any party to the belligerent countries does so at their own risk." President Roosevelt's statement, which does not provide any protection to citizens trading with belligerent countries, is a step further than what is stipulated in the Neutrality Act. Previously, Senators Clark and others had made such a proposal, but it was not passed by Congress. A careful reading of President Roosevelt's remarks indicates that the United States does not want to formally protect cargo ships heading to belligerent countries, does not want to oppose the blockade actions of the League of Nations or any other country, and does not want to insist on the rights of neutral countries to trade. (Reuters dispatch, 5th) The U.S. government's decision to strictly enforce the prohibition of arms shipments to both Italy and Abyssinia has been enthusiastically welcomed by British political circles and various circles of the League of Nations, who feel that this move by the United States has provided important guidance to the Council of the League of Nations and view it as a contribution of "inviting sanctions and the United States not interfering." (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

Berlin Newspapers Observe the East African War Situation, Italian Forces Limited by Geography, Victory is Difficult, Potential for Escalation into British-Italian Conflict

(Berlin) German circles are very interested in the Italo-Abyssinian conflict. Major German newspapers have sent special correspondents to the front lines in Italy and Abyssinia to observe the war. German military experts have many doubts about whether Italy can win, believing that although Italy possesses new-style weapons, the geographical difficulties of Abyssinia will render the new-style weapons ineffective. Some people believe that there is a possibility that Britain and Italy may engage in armed conflict, which would undoubtedly benefit Germany. As for the general German population, they all oppose Italy, believing that it is insufficient to use a country's cultural backwardness as a pretext for attacking it. If that were the case, then in a few years, Germany could also use the fact that France's adoption of a democratic system is more backward than German politics as a pretext to attack France. The Nazi Party also does not approve of Italy, because Mussolini opposes Germany's annexation of Austria. Some Nazi newspapers are very dissatisfied with Italy, believing that Italy's fascism and Germany's National Socialism are not the same. In Europe, Italy's fascist system has a better reputation, so they cannot help but be jealous. However, the Nazi Party is quite pleased that the Anglo-French-Italian united front established by the Stresa Conference has broken down after the Italo-Abyssinian conflict occurred. However, seeing that the relationship between Britain and France is growing stronger, they cannot help but feel regret. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Italian Minister Still Residing in Abyssinian Capital, Constantly Communicating with Rome

(Rome) It is reported that the Italian Minister to Abyssinia, Vinci, is still in the Abyssinian capital, continuing to communicate with Rome via wireless radio. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Hundreds of Japanese Military Officers Go to East Africa, Tokyo Authorities Deny It

(Tokyo) The authorities today formally denied the claim that approximately 100 Japanese military officers have set out for Abyssinia. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

British Warships Continue to Arrive in Hong Kong from Weihaiwei, Future Actions Not Announced

(Hong Kong) The British submarine mother ship Medway, accompanied by several submarines, arrived here this morning from Weihaiwei. Its future actions have not been announced by the authorities. (Reuters dispatch, 6th)

Current Commentary

The Difficult Problem of International Sanctions

— Star

Since its establishment, the League of Nations has never applied the provisions regarding sanctions in Article 16 of the Covenant. In the Manchurian Incident, the League of Nations work ended in a failed mediation due to Britain's unwillingness to take responsibility, and the fact of aggression succeeded. Now that the Italian army has captured Aduwa, and the League of Nations' report has also been published, the work of Article 15 of the Covenant has been completed, and the work of Article 16 must begin. Whether or not to implement sanctions is one question. The extent and scope of implementation is another question. Whether the implementation is effective and whether there are dangers is an even bigger question. Recently, the British side, in order to awaken the attention of France and the United States, expressed its attitude towards this problem. First, it said that if sanctions are implemented, all powerful countries must be included. Second, it said that the implementation of sanctions must not fail due to the actions of non-member states. The former is addressed to France and other countries within the League of Nations, deeply worried that they will adopt the tactic of watching the fire from across the wall or throwing stones down the well. The latter is addressed to the United States and other countries outside the League of Nations, deeply fearing that they will gloat over the misfortune, take advantage of the fire, and profit from the fisherman's gain in the fight over the wall. Britain's situation is difficult, and the weaknesses of the League of Nations have been revealed, and the difficulty of the sanctions problem is also obvious.

According to the provisions of Article 16 of the Covenant, it is to enable Article 10 of the Covenant to maintain its sanctity. The content of Article 10 is that the member states of the League of Nations respect and guarantee the territorial integrity and political independence of each member state. Whether a country is large or small, once it is invaded by another country, the entire League of Nations is responsible for fulfilling this guarantee obligation. Sanctions are the punishment for the aggressor, so that it will be afraid beforehand and regret afterwards. The sanction methods listed in Article 16 are economic sanctions, military sanctions, and political sanctions. Political sanctions are the expulsion of the aggressor from the League of Nations. It does no harm to the aggressor. We can prove it from the past of Japan. Military sanctions have always been opposed by some countries, believing that it is replacing violence with violence, which is not the original intention of peace. Therefore, the Covenant only stipulates that the League of Nations can suggest that certain countries contribute naval, land, and air forces, and that the countries do not stop the transit of international troops. However, whether to contribute or not is the freedom of each country, and there is no obligation to obey. Economic sanctions are the most promising of all sanctions. However, according to the resolutions of previous League of Nations conferences, whether or not each country participates in sanctions is decided by the government of each country. The degree of participation is also not forced. If there are geographical or factual difficulties, they can also be exempted from participation. Seeing this, the powerlessness of the sanction clauses is obvious, and it is difficult to maintain the sanctity of Article 10 with Article 16.

However, the center of gravity of international sanctions is not in the clauses and laws, but in actual politics. First, the world's most powerful countries, such as the United States and Japan, are not members of the League of Nations and have no obligation to maintain the Covenant. Second, the powerful countries within the League of Nations, due to different environments and different security requirements, use the League of Nations as a tool for diplomacy and politics, rather than as an ideal and purpose. Therefore, in the Manchurian Incident, Britain refused the request of the United States by using Japan to value itself. In the Abyssinian problem, France did not have the determination to accept British leadership by using Italy to value itself. Sleeping in the same bed but dreaming different dreams, each is right in its own way. Third, the concept of joint responsibility and collective peace has not yet defeated the concept of national sovereignty supreme. There are more than fifty countries in the world, and there are more than fifty highest wills, each of which considers its own interests as the final decision condition. For example, it is actually impossible for Canada to block Italy or for Norway to assist Abyssinia. Fourth, the interdependence of the economies of various countries is increasing day by day. If Italy is blockaded, many countries that rely on Italy's raw materials and Italy's markets will see increased unemployment and factories closing their doors. Fifth, the cause of war has not been eliminated. Among the imperialist countries, there are satisfied and dissatisfied ones. Among the nationalist countries, there are those who invade other nationalities and those who are invaded by other nationalities. The maintenance of this status quo inevitably has unfair reasons. The sanction provisions are only to maintain this status quo. All these reasons are political in nature and cannot be saved by the modification of clauses or the loyalty of one or two countries.

Page 5

Machang Township, Shuyang County, Flooded, Thousand Acres of Fertile Land Submerged by Floods, Geysers Erupt, West Embankment Sinks Instantly

(Xuzhou) The Shuyang Machang Township Three Mile Embankment collapsed, flooding hundreds of acres of fertile land. Geysers were discovered outside the West Embankment Gate, water gushing out like a waterfall. The ground subsided approximately three to four square zhang. Residents were sprayed by the water into the sky and fell back down. In an instant, the West Embankment sank, houses collapsed, and many people died. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Xuzhou) Machang Township in the Eighth District of Muyang County, due to the breach of the Chaimi Embankment, floodwaters and the Yellow River's current submerged thousands of acres of fertile land. The Machang Embankment has not yet been breached. Yesterday, geysers were discovered in many places within the embankment, suddenly gushing out several inches high. In an instant, the terrain subsided by tens of zhang. People were horrified. Now, the embankment is also sinking. Residents are surrounded by floods outside the embankment and sudden springs within the embankment, with no way to escape. Many have drowned. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 6th)

Canal Embankment in Huaiyin Collapses, Rush to Conscript Laborers for Emergency Repairs

(Qingjiangpu) Huaiyin County Magistrate Dong Zhe, due to the Yellow River's water pouring into Liutang, the water level in Jin Kou, Wangjia Da Chong, Baojia River Mouth, and Xuliu in the county rose sharply, creating an extremely dangerous situation. He specially dispatched technical personnel Liu Pingshi, Wang Yuliang, Jin Jufang, etc., to go with the Fourth and Fifth District Chiefs Wang Xiuliang and Tang Xiaobai, rush to conscript 20,000 laborers to be stationed for emergency repairs. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Qingjiangpu) Feng Dan, director of the Huaipi Section Engineering Office, learned that the embankments on both sides of the canal in the Sanbao area of the Fourth District of Huaiyin County were washed away by water and were in disrepair. Believing that the Yellow River was diverting into the canal, he was afraid that a slight oversight would lead to danger. He has now dispatched Engineer Wu Shijiang to discuss with the county government to conscript laborers for emergency protection. County Magistrate Dong also went to Sanbao to inspect after receiving the report and returned to the city at 7:00. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Qingjiangpu) The water in the Liutang River in Shisayang Zhongxing North Eighteen Li overflowed, causing great panic among merchants and residents in Binhe Shiji. The county government conscripted laborers for emergency repairs. Also, the Zhongyun Canal Embankment next to the South Gate of Zhongxing Town was in danger of collapsing, which would flood the entire town. In recent days, the canal water has risen suddenly, and residents have been unable to sleep peacefully at night. In addition to sending people to guard day and night, they also worshiped the old generals and kings and other reptiles. The incense at Yangqiao North and South is extremely prosperous. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Guanyun Laborers Rush to Repair the East Embankment of the Salt River, Opening up the Da Taiping Sluice to Release Water

(Xuzhou) Haixun, after the sudden rise and breach of the Salt River, the Chaimidingdang Rivers successively breached, and the water flowed straight down into Guanyun and invaded Banpu, the location of the Guanyun County government. The rivers near Banpu are rising daily. The county seat is an earthen embankment. The county government is gathering laborers to repair it. County Magistrate Xu Xiekui is leading 20,000 laborers to rush to repair the East Embankment of the Salt River. If the East Embankment breaches, Guanyun County will be submerged. The Salt Affairs Inspection Office is already surrounded by water, and the situation is critical. Xu plans to move the county seat to the South City if necessary and has sealed hundreds of civilian boats for use. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Xuzhou) Haixun, after the water level in Guanyun Huanghui rose without falling, he investigated the downstream Taiping Sluice of the Salt River and found that the water release was not smooth. He gathered laborers on the spot and widened the sluice gate so that the water could enter the sea from the Shaoxiang River and dredged the Yancha Caoba. The tail gate was completely dredged to ensure smooth discharge. It is hoped that the water level in Guanyun will drop in the future. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Qingjiangpu) The Bian Dan River Jia Gou in the middle of North and South Liutang overflowed this afternoon. Most of the residents of Xiajitan have moved to Huaiyin and Lianshui to avoid the flood. Those near Shangjitan and Nanliutang Fendu Cheng and Houjiazuwai have mostly moved to Qingjiang and other places, leaving only strong men to guard the doors. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Hao Guoxi and Others Discuss Flood Prevention Measures, Shao Hanyuan Goes to the Province to Report on Flood Control Efforts

(Xuzhou) Hai District Commissioner Hao Guoxi, Chief Engineer of the Water Conservancy Association Guan Fuquan, and Engineer Ge Hanlou of the Daohuai Office discussed flood prevention measures in Xinpu. First, dredge the outlet to the sea in Guanpei. Second, build a large waterproof dam in Dongmu to reduce the disaster area. Third, block the breach in the Liutang River so that the eastern water can return to the channel. After Hao and others decided on the measures, they set off for Guanyun to investigate, conscript laborers, and provide guidance. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Xuzhou) Shao Hanyuan, believing that the severe flood period in this area had passed, took the night train south last night with Engineer Yu Shufang of the Construction Department to report to the province on the flood control efforts and to request instructions on thorough relief measures in the future. The disaster in Xu is heavier than in the past. The current and coming winter and spring famine periods are very long and need to be relieved, but the local strength is insufficient and relies on provincial assistance. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Yellow River Closing Project, Re-estimated Funding

(Jinan) The funding for the Yellow River closing project and subsequent expenses was originally estimated to be more than 4.8 million, but due to financial difficulties, it has been re-estimated to be more than 4.4 million, including 2.39 million for the closing project. The closing method is a combination of old and new methods, first driving piles and dragging stones to build a cut-off dam, and finally carrying out the closing. More than ten counties in western Shandong are still a vast ocean, and there is no hope of planting wheat. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Song Discusses and Decides on Security Measures for Beiping and Tianjin

(Beiping) Regarding the jurisdiction of the Ping-Tianjin Garrison Command and the Hebei Security Department, the Military Affairs Commission previously ordered Song Zheyuan and Shang Zhen to coordinate and discuss maintenance measures. It is now learned that Song and Shang have agreed to jointly maintain the area by the 29th and 32nd Armies, without dividing the boundaries. Therefore, the security of Ping, Tianjin, and Gu can be said to be worry-free. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 6th)

(Tianjin) Shang Zhen said that he came to Tianjin to handle the accumulated affairs of the Tianjin-Gu Security Command and to take care of personal matters. Li Haitian has been formally appointed as the commander of the Third Security Brigade stationed in Luan County. Liu Lesan, the cavalry battalion commander of the brigade, has been dismissed and is with Secretary-General Zhang Weixiang in Yuguan. The cavalry battalion has been reduced to a company and is directly under the command of Li Haitian. The candidate for the administrative specialist in the Ji-Mi District has not been determined. The bandit suppression affairs on the Great Wall line are being discussed by Yin Rugeng and Takeshita. Once a solution is found, it will be implemented. The reorganization of Feng Shoupeng's unit and Luo Dongshu's unit has been completed and they have been moved out of Tangshan to their designated defense areas. As winter defense is approaching, the province will implement a divided-area bandit suppression method, with each area sending a regiment to be responsible. The Hebei Province budget has been barely compiled into a total of 57 million, with income and expenses matching. There are two temporary fees of more than 100,000 each for occasional expenses. Shang Zhen plans to host foreign guests in Tianjin and will stay in Tianjin for about a week before returning to Baoding. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Qin Decun Talks About the Tranquility of Eastern Chahar, Zhao Denyu's Division Arrives in the Suburbs of Beiping from Zhangjiakou

(Beiping) Qin Decun arrived in Beiping from Zhangjiakou this morning. According to him, after returning to Zhangjiakou this time, he went to Zhangbei, Chaigoubu, and other places to inspect for several days. The situation in eastern Chahar is tranquil. Luo Dongchu has already arrived in Chahar Province, Yongning Village, and will be reorganized into a security team in the future. The bandits in Yanqing have now been incorporated. After Zhao Denyu was ordered by the Military Affairs Commission to depart, he is now moving to the suburbs of Beiping one after another. Liu Ruming's division will continue to move out after Zhao's unit has completed its departure. He himself will go to Tianjin tonight to visit Song and plans to return to Chahar on the 9th to preside over the Chahar Provincial Civil Service Examination to be held on the 11th. Also, it is reported that Zhao Denyu's division left Zhangjiakou yesterday morning and arrived in the suburbs of Beiping this morning. The rest is being transported one after another and will be able to complete the departure within three days. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Tianjin) The Eastern Chahar Security Team has recently agreed to编4,000 men. In addition to those trained by Chahar Province, the bandit units of Shi Yousan and Liu Guitang are being recruited, 1,000 men from Wangdao's group, plus more than 200 men from Luo Dongshu's unit, to form a brigade and stationed in the area of Yanqing Yongningpu Huikou. Wangdao's group was recently inspected by Wang Shiping, the county magistrate of Yanqing County. Luo Dongshu's unit set out from Shunyi on the 5th and went to Yongningpu to wait for the inspection and reorganization. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Tianjin) Qin Decun arrived at 6:00 PM on the 6th from Chahar. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

The 53rd Army Miao Unit Will Be Transferred to the Ping-Bao Line

(Beiping) After the Ping City Defense and Security was transferred to the 37th Division of the 29th Army by the Ping-Tianjin Garrison Command, the 116th Division Miao Zhengliu Unit of the 53rd Army, originally stationed in the suburbs of Ping, has been ordered by the Military Affairs Commission to be transferred to the Ping-Bao Line. The Miao Unit has been prepared and will depart by train tomorrow to be stationed in Changxindian, Liulihe, Liangxiang, and Yixian. The division headquarters will be located in Liulihe. Miao will leave Ping and go to Liulihe to manage everything after the troops have completed their departure in the next few days. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Two Teams of Feng Shoupeng's Unit Arrive in Changping

(Beiping) Three hundred and seventeen men of the Zhanqu Special Police Force Feng Shoupeng Unit passed through Beiping to Changping last night. Two companies have already entered Changping this morning. One company is stationed in the Bohai area at the junction of Changping and Miyun. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Bandits are Active Again Along the Great Wall, An agreement has been reached with the Japanese side on Bandit Suppression Measures

(Beiping) Yang, a bandit group near Malanyu, has recently been active again. The authorities immediately contacted Takeshita, the head of the Kwantung Army's Yuyu Special Service Agency, to discuss bandit suppression. An agreement has been reached and will be implemented in the next few days. The suppression of Hua Hui opium poison and ronin in the war zone has also been discussed. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Beiping) Zhang Haijiao and Yang Erliang, two bandit groups in the war zone, have reunited and fled into the Great Wall line again. There are bandits from the Zhang Yang alliance in Malanyu, Luo Wenyu, Banbishan, and north of Miyun. Zhang Yantian and Zhang Qingyu, two units of the war zone's security team, are now implementing joint defense. The Japanese troops stationed along the Great Wall line and Sahe Bridge and other places will implement assisting the security team in pursuing and suppressing the bandits after receiving official orders. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

The Dispute in the Luan Prefecture Third Brigade Has Been Resolved, The Mounted Police Have Been Reorganized Into an Infantry Police Company

(Beiping) The dispute that occurred in the Second Security Brigade stationed in Luan County some days ago has been resolved by Yin Rugeng in Tianjin. Brigade Commander Li Haitian can also exercise his powers, and local order is as usual. The mounted police battalion under the brigade will be reorganized into an infantry police company. Battalion Commander Liu Leer is in Yu, and the authorities have ordered him to return to his hometown to retire. Yin Rugeng is scheduled to go to Luan from Tianjin on the 8th to inspect the unit. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 6th)

Fifteen Male and Female Kidnappers in Tianjin Executed, Shot at Wangzhuang Execution Ground

(Tianjin) Fifteen male and female bandits involved in the major kidnapping case in Tianjin were convicted after interrogation by the Tianjin-Gu Security Command. The sentence was submitted to the Military Affairs Commission for approval and was approved early on the 6th. The command immediately took the prisoners Zhang Lianke, Tian Zhangshi, etc. from the prison at 2:00 PM, verified their identities, and escorted them to the Xiaowangzhuang execution ground by a military police battalion to carry out the execution by firing squad. Tens of thousands of Chinese and Western spectators crowded the road during the execution. The bandits asked for wine, food, and cigarettes along the way. They did not arrive at the execution ground until 3:00 PM for execution. Thirteen male and female suspects in the case were released on bail. The bandits had been committing crimes for three years, killing twelve people and extorting 11,000 yuan. The people's hearts were overjoyed after the execution, and the newspapers issued extra editions. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Visited the Sichuan Provincial Government Yesterday, He Visited Dujiangyan for Irrigation on the day before.

(Chengdu) Accompanied by Liu Xiang, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek visited the Sichuan Provincial Government. Liu Xiang retired to the inner room to rest, and Chiang Kai-shek inquired in detail about the internal affairs of the provincial government. After about forty minutes of talk, Chiang accompanied Liu on a week of inspection and then returned to his residence by car. (Central News Agency, 6th)

(Chengdu) In the morning of the 5th, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek visited Qingcheng Mountain and Dujiangyan for irrigation by car, and Chiang Kai-shek praised the project. He returned to the province by car in the afternoon. (Central News Agency, 6th)

Thorough Investigation of West Gong Banner Dispute, Personnel Selection Undecided, It is Said That the Central Government Intends to Send He Jingwu for Mediation, Wu He Reschedules His Trip North to the 8th

(Nanjing) After the Central Government telegraphed both parties to await disposal, the Mongolian side has expressed willingness to wait for the Central Government to resolve the West Gong Banner dispute. The government previously intended to send Yu Feipeng, the Vice Minister of Communications, to Mongolia for thorough investigation, but Yu declined, and it is proposed to change to He Jingwu, the Counselor of the Mongolian Political Guidance Office. A discussion will be held at the Administrative Yuan meeting on the 8th, and a decision can be made after obtaining He's consent. According to Wu Heling, the head of the offices of the leagues and banners stationed in Beijing, I was originally scheduled to go north on the 6th to participate in the Mongolian Political Conference. Now, in order to wait for the central government to decide on the personnel selection, I plan to leave on the 8th. After seeking instructions from President Wang and Minister He on the central government's intention to resolve the West Gong Banner dispute, Wang and He both instructed me to inform both parties that they should obey the central government's fair mediation and it is expected that it can be resolved. The dismissal of Yunwang from the position of Qasake this time is based on his qualifications as the leader of the league, in accordance with the established practices of the Mongolian leagues and banners, and is not related to the eight principles of Mongolian autonomy. (Special Dispatch, 6th)

(Nanjing) Due to Yu Feipeng's firm refusal despite being urged, the personnel selection for the West Gong Banner dispute will be discussed again at this week's Yuan meeting. If Yu firmly refuses, others may be sent instead. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 6th)

Bandit Suppression in Northern Shaanxi: All Units Mobilized

Restriction on Foreign Grain Imports: Executive Yuan Refers to Three Ministries for Review

Ministry of Industry Clarifies the Nature of Processing

(Nanjing) In response to a request from the Wuhan Municipal Government, the Ministry of Industry has issued the following clarification regarding the interpretation of Article 1 of the revised factory registration regulations: "While processing is not manufacturing, the finished product is invariably altered compared to its pre-processed state. Therefore, it should be considered as manufacturing and subject to the provisions of the second paragraph of Article 1 of the factory registration regulations." (Sixth Central News Agency Dispatch)

Public Servants' Relief Donations: Ministry of Finance Transfers to Central Bank Regularly

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has collected salary donations from public servants nationwide, totaling approximately 3.03 million yuan. Except for half of the September donations from some central government departments, which have been fully received, the deductions from the remaining provinces will begin in October and are expected to be fully remitted by the end of December. The Ministry will transfer the deducted or received funds to the Central Bank for storage. The disaster relief agency will manage the allocation of these funds to the disaster areas. (Sixth Dispatch)

Ministry of Interior Replies to Henan Province Regarding Measures to Protect Foreign Missionaries

(Nanjing) In response to an inquiry from the Henan Provincial Government regarding whether there are restrictions on foreigners coming to China to preach, the Ministry of Interior stated that if Chinese nationals affiliated with foreign religious organizations such as Catholic or Protestant churches are found to be violating existing laws under false pretenses, they should be dealt with according to the law. Foreigners coming to China to preach are subject to the "Provisional Regulations on Foreign Churches in the Interior Renting Land and Buildings," but no other restrictions are in place. Furthermore, there is no precedent prohibiting congregations in County A from establishing missions in Counties B and C. However, the local administrative authorities should be consulted beforehand to ensure proper supervision and protection. If a church requests official protection, it may be granted at the discretion of the authorities. This information has been communicated to all provincial and municipal governments for their reference. (Sixth Dispatch)

Therefore, in addition to instructing the Shanghai Banking Association to urge them to comply, the Ministry of Finance is considering stipulating that banks registered elsewhere without the Ministry's approval will not be allowed to operate. Regulations Concerning Transportation for Foreign Diplomats in China

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways has formulated several regulations regarding transportation for ambassadors and ministers from various countries using state-owned railways, and has issued them to all railway bureaus nationwide: 1. Ambassadors traveling to Nanjing to assume or relinquish their posts may have a reserved carriage attached to the train free of charge (excluding the Ping-Hu postal train), but must purchase their own tickets. 2. Ministers traveling to Nanjing to assume or relinquish their posts may reserve two compartments, but must purchase their own tickets (excluding the Ping-Hu postal train and international sleeper cars). 3. Chargés d'affaires traveling to Nanjing to assume or relinquish their posts may reserve one compartment, but must purchase their own tickets (excluding the Ping-Hu postal train and international sleeper cars). 4. Ambassadors, ministers, and chargés d'affaires must pay for their own tickets when traveling to other destinations. Embassy staff members must pay for both carriage and tickets when traveling to other destinations. (Sixth Dispatch)

US and Japan Sign Agreement to Limit Japanese Cloth Exports to the Philippines: Valid for Two Years

(Washington) The United States and Japan have recently signed an agreement regarding the import of cotton textiles into the Philippines. The agreement will be valid for two years and stipulates that the United States and Japan should each account for 50% of the Philippine cotton textile market. Competition between the US and Japan in the Philippine cotton textile market has been intense recently. This agreement between the US and Japan will eliminate a point of conflict in the Pacific. (Fifth Havas Dispatch)

US Airship Makes Another Test Flight Across the Pacific: Vanguard in Opening a Route to the Far East

Alameda, California. The Pan American Airways airship "Clipper" departed today for a test flight to Guam. The flight will pass through Hawaii, Midway Island, and Wake Island. It is widely believed that this is the final test flight. If the results are satisfactory, the Clipper will open a new commercial route from the United States across 8,500 miles of the Pacific Ocean to the Far East. It plans to stop at nine locations: Hawaii, Midway Island, Wake Island, Guam, and the Philippines. Before the Clipper's departure today, the Postal Service, in response to requests from stamp collectors, allowed the airship to carry a special batch of mail, charging $125 per piece. (Fifth Reuters Dispatch)

Reorganization of Sichuan Local Currency Progressing Smoothly

(Nanjing) According to the Ministry of Finance, except for a few areas where bandit suppression military operations are still underway, the financial administration of Sichuan Province has been fully returned to the provincial government. The next issue to be addressed is the reorganization of local currency. The Ministry of Finance is fully transporting Central Government currency to Chengdu for exchange. The process has been progressing smoothly, and it is expected to be completed in two months. To prevent fraud, local currency will be destroyed immediately after being collected. After this, the Central Government currency will be the monetary standard of Sichuan. As for the reorganization of Sichuan coinage, according to a survey by the Provincial Department of Finance, there are a total of 70 million yuan in miscellaneous coins in the province. The complete recall and recoining of the national currency, excluding transportation costs, minting costs, and losses, will result in a loss of over 3 million yuan. It has been agreed that the Sichuan Department of Finance will be responsible, and the Central Mint will handle the minting. There are no other difficulties. The implementation of this recall and recoining plan will begin after the reorganization of local currency is complete. (Sixth Dispatch)

The Mission of the Committee for the Reorganization Plan of the Yuehan Railway

A reporter from the Central News Agency noted that the completion of the entire Yuehan Railway is of great importance to the convenience of traffic on the Yuehan Line and the prosperity of industry, and that the committee bears a great responsibility. They interviewed Xia Guangyu, the chairman of the committee, at the Pacific Hotel in Hankou. According to Xia, the Yuehan Railway, which runs from Wuchang in the north to Guangzhou in the south, is a crucial trunk line in southern China. After the establishment of the National Government, attention was immediately paid to the work of completing the entire line. The Ministry of Railways has made great efforts to complete the remaining project for the Zhushao section using Sino-British Boxer Indemnity funds. After the railway is open to traffic in the future, it is essential that the repayment of principal and interest is fulfilled on schedule to establish credibility. This is crucial for securing funds for future construction of new lines. Therefore, the future of national railway policy is extremely important. In order to achieve this goal, the entire line must generate reliable profits each year after it opens to traffic, sufficient to cover the required repayment of principal and interest. The committee's most important mission is to plan how to develop affairs after the entire line opens to traffic, so that the operating revenue, in addition to maintaining the road, will be sufficient for repayment of principal and interest. Therefore, the transportation organization, engineering, finance, and other aspects of the completed and unified road are all interrelated and must be organized and planned in advance. Prospects of the Italo-Ethiopian War: Staging an Attack on Ethiopia to Maintain Domestic Rule; If the Incident Escalates, Britain and France Will Be the First to Join the Vortex

France's protection of Italy is also related to the previous Anglo-German naval agreement. The Anglo-German naval agreement is tantamount to Britain helping Germany rise and making things difficult for France. Therefore, France's attitude towards the current Italo-Ethiopian dispute seems to disregard British interests. Its ambiguous response to Britain's proposal for a joint front further reveals France's blatant protection of Italy.

(4) What will happen if the incident escalates?

However, if the Italo-Ethiopian war drags on and the incident escalates, and if Britain is drawn into the vortex, then France will inevitably join forces with Britain to jointly restrain Italy.

British diplomacy has always been known as "cunning." If war breaks out between Britain and Italy, and France does not provide assistance, then Britain will also stay out of European continental affairs and focus on dealing with its colonies. If so, the peace mechanism of the European continental bloc will completely collapse, and the Locarno Treaty, which guarantees France, will be torn to shreds. Therefore, in terms of diplomatic principles, France still takes cooperation with Britain to maintain the European status quo as a prerequisite. The possibility of a joint Anglo-French front to restrain Italy is still greater.

The French Foreign Minister once questioned the British Foreign Minister, saying, "Since the British government insists on upholding the League of Nations Covenant, if an act of aggression occurs on the European continent, such as a third country (referring to Germany) invading Austria's independence and peace, will Britain still be able to express its determination at that time?" Commentators also say that France has already allowed assistance if Italy attacks Britain, which is indeed believable. In short, if Britain is drawn into the vortex of the Italo-Ethiopian war, France will inevitably take action immediately. Although the Italo-Ethiopian war may not directly trigger a European war, it will undoubtedly become the cause of future European chaos. Observing Germany's silence and Italy's reckless behavior, one can be convinced.

(1) The Inevitability of Italy's Attack on Ethiopia

The Italo-Ethiopian war has already broken out. Tracing back to its origin, it is said that it was caused by Italy's attempt to conquer Abyssinia. Judging from Abyssinia's attitude of bowing its head and listening to Britain's proposal to the League of Nations for a peaceful resolution before the conflict, Abyssinia has in fact become a territory under international joint administration since 1906, when Britain, France, and Italy divided their spheres of influence in Abyssinia. Concessions have reached the extreme, but why is Italy determined to conquer Abyssinia this time?

Based on reports from all sides and the internal contradictions within Italy, it can be seen that Italy's attack on Ethiopia has reasons: (1) Italy lacks natural resources and faces a population problem due to a lack of imperialism, so it needs to implement a national expansion policy to plunder colonies; (2) Abyssinia is the most suitable destination for Italy to obtain resources and establish relationships; (3) In recent years since the establishment of the Italian regime, financial and economic loopholes have repeatedly appeared, and high-pressure policies have been gradually adopted towards the people, leading to growing popular resentment. Mussolini intends to divert public attention by waging war abroad; (4) Mussolini wants to increase the people's faith in him, instigate the Italian people's idea of revenge by using the defeat in the Ethiopian war more than 30 years ago, and colonize Ethiopia; (5) Since Germany withdrew from the League of Nations, the European balance of power has been disrupted. In order to counter Germany, France has to compromise with Italy, making this the best time for Italy to conquer Ethiopia.

Italians have been preparing for more than a year since they decided to attack Ethiopia. The military expenditure spent in the past year has reached 800 million lira, and the dispatched forces have also reached 200,000. As a result, the financial deficit continues to increase, and export trade is gradually declining. Therefore, Mussolini used colonization policies, national expansion, racial struggles, and the recovery of the defeat at Adowa as pretexts for attacking Ethiopia. In fact, there is another inevitability.

(2) Italy's Attack on Ethiopia and Britain

The biggest obstacle to Italy's attack on Ethiopia is Britain. The reason why Italy has hesitated for so long is also because it does not know how to deal with Britain. However, Britain opposes Italy's attack on Ethiopia on the grounds that Italy's act of aggression directly undermines the peace mechanism of the European group. At the League of Nations Council meeting on September 4, British representative Eden repeatedly stated that he was willing to uphold the League of Nations' principles of peace and mediate the Italo-Ethiopian dispute. In fact, the League of Nations is nothing more than an agency for Britain and France. If it can uphold peace, how could the Sino-Japanese dispute have occurred?

The reason why Britain is unwilling to attack Ethiopia is that its own territory borders Ethiopia. Preserving Ethiopia's formal independence is to safeguard its colonial interests in the Philippines. Judging from the geographical situation of Abyssinia, it can be seen that Abyssinia is surrounded by the colonies of Britain, France, and Italy, and the interests of the three countries in Abyssinia are extremely complex. In the mid-19th century, when Abyssinia leased Somaliland and Eritrea to Italy, Italy had almost exclusive rights in Abyssinia. Later, through the 1906 treaty between Britain, France, and Italy, Abyssinia became a sphere of equilibrium for the three countries, which was also a move by Britain and France to jointly contain Italy. Today, Britain's attitude towards Italy is still to maintain its inherent influence in Abyssinia.

In 1923, when France brought Abyssinia into the League of Nations, we still remember Britain's expression of opposition. The reasons it held were exactly the same as Mussolini's derogatory remarks about Abyssinia today, saying that Abyssinia is a barbaric country with a slave system. How can it be included among the civilized countries of the League of Nations? The words are still in my ears. Is it that the British people are forgetful? In particular, Britain is unwilling to attack Ethiopia. If Italy wins Abyssinia, Britain's interests in Abyssinia will be in jeopardy. If Abyssinia does not win, the colonies of Britain in the Philippines will continue to resist, and it will also be enough to influence the resistance consciousness of other small and weak ethnic groups in British colonies, which is all unfavorable to Britain. What Britain wants is to maintain the status quo.

(3) Italy's Attack on Ethiopia and France

To further elaborate on France's attitude towards the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, we must first understand the nature of France's interests in Ethiopia. France's interests in Ethiopia are different from those of Italy and Britain. Italy has a railway between its territory Eritrea and Italian Somaliland, initially wanting to seize Abyssinia's mineral resources, and then wanting Abyssinia to become Italy's protectorate. Britain cultivates cotton in Egypt and Sudan along the Nile River as a supply of raw materials for Britain's cotton industry. The irrigation of Kamsu relies on water from the Nile, and the discharge of the Nile originates from Lake Tana in Ethiopia. If the water source of Lake Tana is cut off, Britain's Egyptian-Sudanese region will become barren land. Therefore, Britain's contention for rights in Ethiopia is also fierce. However, France's attitude towards Ethiopia is different. France already has an exclusive railway in Ethiopia, and the path to cultural facilities and development in Ethiopia is still far away. France is not as active in Ethiopia as Italy and Britain, but it does not want Ethiopia to be exclusively occupied by Italy or Britain.

France is deeply troubled by Germany. Since Hitler came to power, it has felt increasingly uneasy. Therefore, its concern for colonies can be said to be secondary to its concern for the European continent. Since Germany withdrew from the League of Nations, revived its military, and attempted to merge with Austria, France has been extremely sensitive and alarmed by Germany's every move. Therefore, regarding the current Italo-Ethiopian dispute, it is said that Italy has long obtained France's understanding. This is also due to France's policy towards Germany, which has led it to protect Italy.

After the Outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War; The Impact on Shanghai's Industry and Commerce; Cotton Yarn and Steel Prices Rise; Raw Silk Exports Sharply Decrease

Xin Sheng News Agency reports: Since the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War, people are terrified of the tragic nature of the previous European War. Those who are nervous almost believe that the second world war will follow one after another. Therefore, it has a great impact on Chinese industrialists and businessmen. The Xin Sheng News Agency reporter recorded the significant changes that have already occurred in various industries:

Cotton yarn: In recent days, the yarn and cotton market has been affected by the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War. Foreign telegrams have reported price increases every day. The Shanghai Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange believes that the import of American cotton has decreased, and the price has also risen. It is found that raw cotton is an indispensable raw material for military supplies, and countries are competing to purchase it. It once rose by 40 pounds a ton the day before. However, the cotton produced in my country is not suitable for spinning fine yarn because its fibers are short and can only be used to spin coarse yarn, so it is difficult to abandon foreign cotton. Moreover, the weather has turned cold in recent days, and customers from all over the world are very enthusiastic about purchasing cotton yarn, which has led to a shortage of現 yarn and a price increase. Shenxin is the largest yarn factory in my country, with the most branches and a large output. It had previously stopped trading due to a shortage of 現 goods. According to yarn industry observers, given the current旺 situation, yarn factories that have stopped work and reduced work will be able to gradually return to their original state.

Steel: The steel菐 market has been sluggish since the spring of this year. Rongda, Maofeng, Renji, and others have successively gone bankrupt. The current prices of various goods have fallen by one yuan and several 角 compared with the spring. After the public meeting decided to stop ordering goods, three months later, due to the scarcity of goods in the market and the tense situation in Italy and Ethiopia, it began to be slightly firm. Since the news of the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War came, people in the industry, in view of the profiteering of the steel industry during the First World War, the market atmosphere suddenly became firm and昂, and the opening price soared by one yuan and as many as three or five 角, and there was still no intention to sell, which caused the iron market to fall into a chaotic state. It is feared that once Britain and France are drawn into the vortex, the steel in the Suez Canal will also be one of the embargoed items. In Japan, steel has also been reported to have risen by 20 yuan a ton. However, in Europe and the United States, in addition to charging military insurance fees, there has been no news of price increases.

Raw silk: Autumn silk in various parts of Jiangsu and Zhejiang has been put on the market one after another, but the output is sharply reduced compared with spring silkworms. Silk merchants buy and pull prices higher than spring silkworms. Since the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War, foreign firms stationed in Shanghai that purchase Chinese silk from Europe and the United States have not dared to抛 buy futures Chinese silk. At the same time, foreign shipping companies have raised the freight rates for Chinese silk imported from China to Europe and the United States from October 1, restoring the previous price of US$4 per piece from US$1.2. As a result, raw silk exports have sharply decreased compared with last month. The silk price of B grade is about 500 yuan in national currency per dan. Therefore, the future of Chinese silk cannot be predicted for a while.
