Factory Fire Inspection: The Shanghai South District Has Been Completed; The Zhabei Districts Will Continue

The Ta Kung News Agency reports: The Municipal Public Security Bureau's factory fire inspection has been carried out very carefully since it began in July of this year, so the progress has been rather slow. The Shanghai South District has only recently been completed. According to the person in charge of the Bureau, based on observations of the inspected factories in the South City, the buildings of the factories are mostly simple and the equipment is incomplete, which is not suitable for establishing factories. Moreover, more than 75% do not comply with building regulations, such as building lofts and converting houses into factory buildings, etc., which is very detrimental to public safety. And the fire-fighting equipment is particularly neglected, and fires are very easy to occur. The focus of the Bureau's fire inspection is on this. However, due to the current economic downturn, in order to be considerate of business difficulties, for the building part, if there is no excessive danger, they are ordered to be careful to protect themselves at any time without being banned. However, those with significant dangers, such as reed mats, waste wood, etc., are ordered to be demolished and cleaned up, and fire-fighting equipment, such as foam fire extinguishers and Taiping faucets, are also required to be installed. The inspection of the Shanghai South District has only been completed recently because there are more factories in the district. After this, Zhabei, Shanghai West, Pudong, and other districts will continue to be held until the inspection is completed.

Before the Administrative Penalty for Navigation is Decided, the Shipping Company Can First Handle the Navigation Procedures; It Will Be Implemented Nationwide from Today with the Approval of the Ministry.

In order to facilitate the business of shipping companies, the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau plans to allow shipping companies to obtain a guarantee from the shop that they will be available at any time to handle the navigation procedures for administrative penalty cases under the Shipping Law, so as to avoid delays and losses. It has been submitted to the Ministry of Communications for review, and the Ministry has now approved it for implementation. The original text is recorded below: Order No. 438 of the Ministry of Communications: "According to the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau's report, 'According to the report of the Ningbo Office, the Bureau forwarded the Ministry of Communications Shipping Vessel No. 3506 order, which stated that administrative penalty cases concerning the Shipping Law should be handled by the court in accordance with the example of penalties for company violations, so as to be uniform, etc., and forwarded it to the Bureau for disposal. Upon receipt of this, the Office has already complied with it. However, it is found that the judicial organs handle cases with troublesome procedures, often delaying for days. If administrative penalty cases concerning the Shipping Law must be handled after the court has completed the procedures before the navigation procedures can be handled, it will definitely take up time, and the shipping company will suffer losses. In order to facilitate the business of the shipping company, the Office will allow the shipping company to obtain a guarantee from the shop that they will be available at any time to handle the over-navigation procedures for administrative penalty cases concerning the Shipping Law. It has been quite convenient for a month. Court procedures are uniform throughout the country, and shipping companies in other places are not without the same pain. A special document is prepared for review and forwarding,' etc. It is found that the above-mentioned method is still feasible if it is approved. It is proposed that when such cases occur in the future, in addition to being transferred to the court for review, the shipping company should also be ordered to provide a guarantee and release them, and at the same time, report to the higher authorities for record-keeping, so as to prevent abuses,'" etc. It is found that the various sections reported are still feasible. In the future, for administrative penalty cases concerning the Shipping Law, in addition to being transferred to the court for review, a reliable guarantee should be obtained for advance release, and it is stipulated that if these cases are handled by the Shipping Administration Bureau or directly transferred to the office, they should be reported to the Ministry at the same time. If they are handled by the Shipping Administration Bureau office, they should be reported to the Ministry at the same time through the Shipping Administration Bureau under its jurisdiction for review and record-keeping. In addition to issuing orders separately, you are hereby ordered to comply with them. This order.

The Fisheries Protection Office of the Ministry of Industry, considering that the autumn fishing season is approaching and fishermen from various regions are flocking to the fishing areas to catch fish, is afraid that pirates will harass the fishermen. Lawyer's Clerk Accused of Perjury

Yu Chunfang, a clerk in a certain law firm, is suspected of giving false testimony in the lawsuit between Dong Wenwei and Yang Shansong. The First Special District Court discovered this and Tang, the prosecutor of the court's inspection office, began investigating. It has now been concluded, and Yu has been prosecuted for perjury in accordance with Article 168 of the Criminal Law. Dong had previously sued Yang in the Second Special District Court for failing to repay a guaranteed loan. After the judgment was final, Yu Chunfang suddenly told Yang that the seals of the four characters "中華蛋廠" (Zhonghua Egg Factory) on the IOU were forged, causing Yang to file a criminal lawsuit against Dong. After investigation, it was found that Yu's testimony in court was false, so he was prosecuted. Yesterday afternoon, the judge of the First Special Court opened a court session to summon and interrogate Yu. First, Prosecutor Tang stated the intention of the prosecution, and then the court asked Yu in detail about the facts of the case. Finally, Yu's defense lawyer made a defense. As a result, Yu Chunfang was ordered by the court to pay a guarantee of 500 yuan, and the actual judgment will be made on Saturday afternoon.

Robberies Are Frequent on the Road Beside Yinggong Temple

Li Wang, a local woman residing on Lafayette Road in the French Concession, collected 60 yuan in association fees at about 8:00 PM the night before last. While walking on the road south of Qingjietang Yinggong Temple on Penglai Road in the city, she was overtaken and robbed by thugs. The woman refused to give up and resisted. The thieves became angry, took out sharp knives, stabbed the woman's right arm, and shed blood all over her body. They also punched the woman to the ground and snatched all the money she was holding in her hand and fled. The woman was knocked unconscious, and passers-by woke her up, but the robbers were gone. The woman immediately reported to the nearby Wenmiao Road Police Station for investigation and arrest, and then went to Qu Zhifu Hospital to sew up and bandage the wound. There are many side roads in the middle of the road at Yinggong Temple, and the robbers can easily escape with the stolen goods. Especially at night, there are few pedestrians, so robberies often occur. Although there are posts in between, there is a sense of being able to take care of one but not the other. I hope that those in power will pay attention to this.

Record of the Shaoxing Wine Industry Association Meeting

The Shaoxing Wine Industry Association of this city held its 27th joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees yesterday. The committee members present were Fang Changsheng, Song Zizhengrong, Wang Zhiqiang, Zhou Jinrong, Chen Jingyun, Xie Jinkui, and other eleven people. Zhou Jinrong chaired the meeting. The agenda items were reported and proposed as usual: (1) The association's annual recurring fee collection case for the 25th year was resolved. If the original place can collect it, it will remain the same; otherwise, the second step will be carried out. (2) After the new stamp tax law was implemented on September 1st, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued two kinds of stamp tax laws and implementation rules. It was resolved that the association should extract and print various legal interpretations and distribute them to members for reference to avoid misunderstandings and penalties. (3) A small number of members of the association resisted paying membership fees. It was resolved that the person in charge should be sent to urge them to pay. If they still refuse to pay, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce will be reported to handle it in accordance with the Ministry of Industry's No. 378 approval. (4) Tongye in Pudong stockpiled good and bad wine from the era of public sales. Recently, the sub-bureau forwarded a letter from the provincial bureau, requiring the new and old to be tied together and resolved at the same time. It was resolved that since Tongye's new certificate wine has been taxed and a new certificate has been obtained, the procedures have been completed, and it is still not allowed to be sold freely. Tongye has no way to sell all the good and bad wine from the era of public sales. How can they suffer losses again? It is unfair. It was resolved to submit a report to the higher-level tax authorities for flexible handling. If it is not approved, further requests will be made. (5) Wang Zhiyu recently transported Chen Shihe's wine jars and was seized by the South Station Inspection Office. The association has already explained the reasons and certified them, but they have not been released. It was found that Wang Zhiyu's wine was indeed taxed and the production, sales, and transportation documents were complete. It was decided to release them after a local investigation to relieve business difficulties and suppress grievances. The above five cases were unanimously passed and the meeting was adjourned.

Cui Tongyue Sold Books to Help with the Account

Mr. Cui Tongyue is a revolutionary veteran. In the past, he promoted the revolution overseas and made remarkable achievements. Today (the 6th) is his seventy-second birthday. Relatives, friends, and old friends celebrated his birthday. Cui, feeling deeply about the severe flood this year, generously donated his book "Canghai Manuscripts" to help with the disaster relief. According to his own statement, "I returned to China for the second time from the United States on April 19th of the 21st year and stayed in Shanghai. Because I was engaged in education and journalism, I once ran the "Minzu" and "Chunqiu" weekly magazines after arriving in Shanghai. At the end of the period, I voluntarily stopped publishing due to direct writing and changed to the position of training and history professor at Jinan University. Suddenly, a student riot occurred, and I avoided it by traveling to the Philippines for several months. Occasionally, friends or students would invite me to tutor Chinese for free. Recently, I wrote "Canghai's Life" in two volumes, which briefly describes my personal experience in the three revolutions in Guangzhou in the years of Yiwei, Gengzi, and Renyin. After fleeing, I founded the "World Public Welfare Daily", "Huaying Daily", and "Youth China Morning Post", all of which vigorously promoted the revolution before the Xinhai Revolution, offending teachers and friends. The Party and the country are inevitable. I ask myself that my sin is unforgivable, let alone meritorious. Now, I am very ashamed to be celebrated by comrades. I would like to donate the book price and remaining expenses to relieve hungry and cold compatriots. I think everyone will understand. My second son, Ailiang, and eldest daughter, Aihuan, live in the countryside and farm. My fourth daughter, Aihua, is studying liberal arts at Columbia University in New York. My fifth son, Zhenqiu, is currently the captain of the 12th Gendarmerie Team in Guangzhou. My sixth daughter, Aiying, is ten years old and is studying in a Guangdong middle school. Together with my wife, Jiang Su, we live a simple family life at No. 1 Sanyili, Chuan Highway, North Shanghai."

Cui Tongyue

A Handgun Was Recovered from the River Under Xinzha Bridge; Niece-in-law of Qian Guisheng Summoned for Questioning

The former residence of Qian Guisheng (deceased), the former mayor of Zhabei, at No. 63 Changan Road, Zhabei, discovered a six-round pistol and 19 bullets in a kerosene tank when demolishing a loft the day before yesterday. The female owner, surnamed Sui, fearing an accident, wrapped them in a cloth bag and had the maid tie them with bricks and sink them under Xinzha Bridge to destroy the evidence. Unexpectedly, the Xinzha Branch Bureau learned of this and sent detectives to hire a boat to recover them and summoned the deceased Qian Guisheng's niece-in-law, Sui, 53 years old, a local, and the maid, Zhang Chen, 52 years old, from Changshu, to the bureau for questioning.

Police Receive Reports from Three Locations: Handwriting of Extortion Letters is the Same; Four People Already Arrested

The Wang family at 50 Wutong Street in the city received successive threatening extortion letters with harsh language. The Wang family ignored them. Unexpectedly, in the last letter received a few days ago, they were asked to send a representative wearing a blue short jacket, a sash, and a duckbill cap to negotiate in the Yuanlong Lane of Manli Bridge between 9 and 10 pm. The Wang family had no choice but to take the letter to the local Yimiao Police Station for investigation. After Police Chief Liu examined the threatening letter, which referred to the Wang family as the former employer, Police Chief Liu personally led Inspector Qiang Zhide, along with patrol officer and police officers in disguise, and armed themselves secretly to lie in ambush. They waited for several nights without any results. Unexpectedly, the Zhou family at 2 Yuanyuan Lane, Lujiazhai, inside Xiaoshumen, also received several similar threatening extortion letters. The last letter instructed Zhou to wrap banknotes in white paper and place them at the entrance of Sunjia Lane on East Street at 10 pm the previous night. Zhou also took the letter to the Yimiao Police Station, requesting a strict investigation. Police Chief Liu observed that the handwriting of the extortion letters was the same as those received by the Wang family. Therefore, they disguised themselves and went to guard and arrest the culprit. At the appointed time, they saw a scrap collector picking up the paper package and fleeing. The detectives surrounded and captured him. He was immediately taken to the station. According to the scrap collector, named Xiao Zhenjiang, he was instructed by Xiao Liuzi and others who were drinking tea at a teahouse at Xinmatou, to pick it up for two jiao (cents), and did not know what was inside the package. Detectives were then ordered to point out and arrest them, and three people were indeed arrested. They are currently under interrogation. It is also heard that a certain family under the jurisdiction of the Xundaostreet Police Station also received a similar threatening extortion letter and is also under investigation.

Yuan Xiangmin Attempts Suicide After Something Goes Wrong

At around 12 noon yesterday, the staff of the Tianran Hotel at 66 Zhifu Road discovered that Yuan Xiangmin, a 25-year-old Ningbo traveler staying in room 216 on the upper floor of the hotel, had not yet gotten up. They instructed the tea boy to knock on the door and call him, but there was no response for a long time. Realizing something was wrong, they managed to open the door and found Yuan Xiangmin lying unconscious on the side of the bed, his face pale and foaming at the mouth. They immediately reported it to the police station and sent him to the hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the poisoning was not severe, and he gradually regained consciousness after treatment. According to Yuan, he used to work as a sample maker at a factory in Hangzhou, but was later dismissed due to some reason. He then came to Shanghai to make a living and currently lives at 1 Hengde Lane, 1 Hengtong Road, Zhabei. However, he has not achieved anything so far, and his financial situation has deteriorated, forcing him to resort to this measure.

Female Suspect in Counterfeit Banknote Case Arrested

Xiao Guangrong, from Shandong, runs a small cigarette and paper shop at 3, Lane 922, East Broadway Road. Last month, a child from Henan tried to exchange a fake one-yuan banknote from the Zhongnan Bank at his shop. The fraud was discovered on the spot, but the child was very alert and fled, abandoning the banknote. On the morning of the 2nd of this month, at around 9 am, Lin Dengen, from Haizhou, used a similar fake banknote to exchange for silver coins and was arrested by Chinese Detective Yin Zhanqing of the Huishan Police Station. Two fake one-yuan banknotes from the Zhongnan Bank and one ten-yuan banknote from China were also found during the search. He was taken to the police station. Upon questioning, the source of the counterfeit banknotes was traced to Hu Wang, a woman from Anhui, at 404 Beijingjiang Road, Zhabei. Detective Yin rushed there, and together with detectives from the Public Security Bureau, arrested Hu Wang and took her to the bureau for detention. The details of Lin's case, after being sent to the First Special District Court, have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the police station obtained an official letter from the court, took Hu Wang back, and sent her to Attorney Li Zhishan of the Industrial Bureau's Criminal Court Three, who presented the case and requested a joint hearing. Hu Wang stated that she had known Lin Dengen for many years. Last November, his wife borrowed ten yuan from her. When her son asked for it back, they argued and fought, resulting in a grudge and false accusation. She claimed to know nothing about the fake banknotes and asked for justice. Presiding Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered her to be remanded in custody and scheduled a joint trial with Lin Dengen at a later date.

Commemorating the Literary Master: Zeng Mengpu Memorial Service Held in Yu, Participants from All Walks of Life, Simple Chariot and White Horses, a Grand Occasion

Mr. Zeng Mengpu of Qinchuan was a literary master. His writings and translations totaled hundreds of volumes. Unfortunately, he passed away in June this summer due to overwork. Individuals who had old friendships with Mr. Zeng in Suzhou, Shanghai, Beijing, and Wuhan, as well as people from academic, political, business, and scholarly circles, and various academic organizations, initiated a memorial service at Yushan to commemorate him. Approximately 500 individuals and 30-40 organizations were listed as participants. The memorial service was held yesterday (Double Ninth Festival) at Xiaoyao You (located at the foot of Yushan) in Changshu. The ceremony was solemn, and the attendees were filled with sorrow when remembering this literary figure. The details are as follows:

Arrangement of the Venue: The memorial service venue was a four-sided hall with substantial space. The East Boat Hall served as a rest area for guests. Mourning couplets and elegies were hung inside and outside the hall and along the corridors. A portrait of Mr. Zeng was hung in the center of the hall, lifelike and full of passion. About forty people lingered around. Wreaths were placed around the portrait. A floral archway was erected at the entrance of Xiaoyao You. A bamboo cloth horizontal plaque was hung above the archway at the Fudi of Yushan. The arrangement was solemn and simple.

Memorial Ceremony: Some participants from Shanghai arrived in Yu the day before. At about 10:00 AM on the morning of the day, the guests (all representatives and leaders from all walks of life) arrived and took their seats. The public memorial ceremony began: (1) Everyone stood at attention; (2) The chief mourner (presumed to be Zhang Zhongren from Wuxian) took his place; (3) Playing mourning music; (4) Performing the sacrificial rite (three bows); (5) Offering flowers; (6) Silent mourning; Reading elegies: First, the chief mourner read the public memorial elegy, followed by Li Haoran representing Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, Shishi Xinbao, Shibao, Chen Bao, Min Bao, Zhonghua Ribao, and Da Wanbao, Shao Xunmei representing Shanghai Times Book Company, and Feng Wuchang and Wu Qiqian reading elegies; (7) Playing mourning music; (8) Ceremony concluded. Subsequently, the memorial service was held: (1) Everyone stood at attention, (2) Playing mourning music, (3) Three bows to the national flag and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, (4) The chairman (Zhang Zhongren) respectfully read Sun Yat-sen's will, (5) The chairman reported the significance of the meeting and a brief biography of the deceased, (6) Representatives from all walks of life, including Yan Duhe, Jiang Zifan, Bao Tianxiao, Zhu Dexuan, Chen Yingsun, and Xu Weinan, delivered speeches, (7) The Zeng family delivered a response, (8) Meeting adjourned.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Zhang Zhongren, over seventy years old, with silver hair, was still full of energy. Mr. Mengpu had a deep friendship with him during his lifetime. During the Jiang-Zhe war, they both resented the tyranny of the warlords and the devastation of the people. They advocated to end the war and exerted themselves for peace. Therefore, he had a deep understanding of Mr. Mengpu's political views. In his report, he cited facts to show Mr. Zeng's diligence in politics and integrity in conduct. In literature, he also praised Mr. Zeng as a representative figure of the transition period between the old and the new. The following speeches were delivered by the representatives, with the general meaning that the gentleman's ethics, politics, morality, learning, and all aspects were worthy of admiration and imitation. Yan Duhe used the three words Zhen (truth), Mei (beauty), and Shan (goodness) (Mr. Zeng ran the Zhenmeishan Bookstore in his later years) to describe the gentleman's personality, which was especially appropriate.

Three Proposals: Mr. Xu Weinan made three proposals: (1) Based on the precedents of foreign literary giants such as Tolstoy, Hugo, Goethe, and Shakespeare, he requested that Mr. Zeng's family retain the original state of the house, furniture, books, and other items used by Mr. Zeng in his daily life as a memorial room, open to the public for exhibition and mourning; (2) He proposed to organize a committee to publish Mr. Zeng's collected works; (3) He proposed to invite artists to cast a bronze statue of Mr. Zeng.

Family Response: Mr. Zeng Yunbai, Mr. Zeng's son, gave a speech of thanks to the guests, saying, "Today, I would like to express my sincere gratitude to all the guests for participating in the joint memorial service for my late father. On the other hand, I am privately delighted to discover for the first time the greatness of my late father's spirit. It is difficult to avoid the change, the death, but there are still many people who remember him, which shows that his spirit will always exist. Everything he did in his life will always remain imprinted in the minds of many people, especially in the minds of our brothers, who can inherit his legacy."

Mourning Couplets and Elegies: The reporter hurriedly excerpted a few of the mourning couplets as follows: (1) "In the past, we were together during eventful times. We shared worries and difficulties, and we still relied on the sick man to save the East Mountain. Now that you have passed away, who will ask about the West Garden?" (Han Zishi). (2) "With a long talent for saving the world, you turned to writing to express your extraordinary spirit. Thinking of your family, you became seriously ill, enduring the pain of recalling old visits to the garden." (Zhang Zhongren). (3) "The sea of sin is a satire of the strange, a complete illusion. You should realize that everything is like a dream. The remnant poems of the Liao River are gone, returning to the pure land. After thirty years of friendship, everything is like smoke." (Chen Taoyi). (4) "Your writing was truly brilliant. The unofficial history compiled and transmitted the Karmic Bonds of Sinful Affairs. An elder has passed away, and literary masters have admired Yushan for thousands of years." (Liu Yazi). (5) "Your writing is as difficult as two things, like pearls and jade joined together. The rise and fall of a generation will be passed down from household to household in the Flowers in a Sea of Sin." (Zhu Yingpeng). Due to space limitations, the rest are omitted. The public memorial elegy is as follows: "Alas, Mr. Zeng, is your life over? The world is in pain, and our party laments. Only you, in your early years, surpassed the group in writing. You were also proficient in textual research, continuing the Han Dynasty's literary works. You occasionally used your spare skills to dabble in novels. The completion of The Sea of Karma was praised as a masterpiece. You wrote strategies and analyzed problems, and your writing was concise. Famous public officials and dignitaries invited you. You went out to govern, and you were in charge of the West Lake. You lingered on poetry and wine, following in the footsteps of Bai Juyi and Su Shi. You were eloquent in the parliament. You worked hard to plan the provincial affairs. Your writings were profound and broad, encompassing the Wei, Jin, Sui and Tang dynasties, eliminating all flowery language. Your political affairs followed the general outline, eliminating disturbances and resolving grievances, enriching the wealth and benefiting the people. Before the measures were halfway through, you suddenly gave up your responsibilities. The people's expectations were high, but Dongshan will not come again. Your conduct was both open and closed, and your circumstances were both frugal and abundant. Is it fate or luck, heaven or man? Those who come to mourn you, who do not sigh? Your successors, like phoenixes and phoenixes, with jade rings and earrings, overlapping and shoulder to shoulder. In your later years, you closed your doors and swept the ground, planting bamboo and eating flowers, leisurely enjoying old age. Alas, my lord, who can live forever? Moreover, in this year of great change, hardship is just beginning. The great men are not those of today. The writings in the famous mountains are enough for thousands of years. Who can do this immortal cause but you? It is enough, what is there to grieve? Only we, your colleagues, have a noble relationship with you. When the shocking news came, we were all surprised. Ashamed of those dignitaries, we falsely claimed to be dead friends, and hurried to the funeral with white horses and plain carriages. Alas, you are gone now, where is your spirit? In the body of Yin and Yang, we offer meager offerings with sincerity, a bundle of grass, a cup of wine. The love is deep but the gifts are meager, the tears are exhausted and the voice is hoarse. We remember your spirit as if you were here, and we hope that you will enjoy this ascent and descent. Alas, alas, I hope you..."

Municipal Public Security Bureau Plans to Build Police Cemetery, Budget Set at Over 30,000 Yuan, Construction to Begin This Month and be Completed Next Spring

According to Dagongshe, the former director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Mr. Wen Hongen, believed that there were many police officers in the bureau who had died in the line of duty over the years, and most of them were from other provinces, so it was very difficult to transport them back to their hometowns for burial. Therefore, he planned to build a police cemetery. However, Mr. Wen died of illness, and the director who succeeded him, Mr. Wen Chaoji, held the position for a short time and did not have time to realize this plan. Now, Director Cai believes that this plan would greatly benefit the police officers of the bureau and is feasible, so he has submitted a request to the Municipal Government to allocate funds and actively prepare for construction. It has now purchased more than 30 acres of land west of Huangjia Garden in Caoking District as the cemetery site. The cemetery plan was designed by architect Dong Dayou. The front is the cemetery road, leading directly to the cemetery gate, then the stele pavilion, followed by Bing Hall, and finally the cemetery. The cemetery can bury more than 1,000 people, surrounded by walls. The entire project will be constructed with steel, cement, Sanhe soil, artificial stone, and other materials. The estimated budget is over 30,000 yuan. More than 20,000 yuan has already been spent on purchasing the cemetery land, and there are still more than 10,000 yuan left. The bureau had previously announced to various construction companies to bid for the construction, and seven companies responded to the bidding. However, the prices they quoted were too high, so the bureau is still considering them. A decision can be made within the week, and construction can begin this month. It is expected that it will be completed in early spring next year.

Man and Woman Attempt Suicide at Far East Hotel Yesterday, Minor Poisoning Not Fatal, Extravagant Behavior Suggests Upper Class

Around 4 PM the day before yesterday, a tragic case of a husband and wife attempting suicide occurred at the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road in this city. The details are as follows: On the 4th of this month, a man named Wu Yaoting, claiming to be from Guangdong, 30 years old, a banker, and his wife, about 20 years old, checked into room 318 on the third floor of the hotel. They usually wore beautiful clothes and behaved very extravagantly, always using a car for transportation. At 1 PM the day before yesterday, the tea boy routinely asked them if they still needed the room. At that time, Wu and his wife showed no signs of abnormality, and asked the tea boy to wait a little longer before making a decision on whether to renew the room. Around 4 PM, the tea boy went to ask again, but found that room 318 was tightly closed, and there was no response when he called. Realizing something was wrong, he managed to pry open the door, and saw that Wu and his wife had both taken poison, their faces pale. He reported it to the accountant, who called Renji Hospital, and the hospital sent an ambulance to transport Wu and his wife to the hospital for treatment. After the incident, a search of the room found no suicide note, only an empty aspirin bottle, and no other drugs. It is said that the poisoning was not deep and there was no danger to their lives. According to the hotel staff, Wu had often booked rooms there. Judging from his usual behavior, he could be considered an upper-class person. It is not known why he attempted suicide this time.

French Concession Public Works Bureau Issues Emergency Notice to Clear Garbage, Corrects Information in Russian Newspaper

Piedian, the acting general manager of the Shanghai French Concession Public Works Bureau, issued an emergency notice yesterday regarding the clearance of garbage, stating: "Notice is hereby given regarding several issues concerning the clearance of garbage in the private streets and lanes of the French Concession. There is erroneous information in the Russian weekly newspaper. This notice is hereby issued so that the public is aware. The garbage clearance regulations of this bureau, since the promulgation of the order No. 122 of the French Consul General's Office on July 30, 1932, have not been modified in any way. All garbage on the public roads in the concession is cleared by the bureau free of charge. As for the residents in the private streets and lanes, in addition to moving their garbage cans to the sidewalks next to the public roads, they enjoy the same treatment as the residents along the public roads. However, if the landlords in the private streets and lanes specifically request the bureau to clear the garbage on their property, they should pay a handling fee once every six months. The fee should be equal to four percent of the total monthly rent of all the houses in that area. Since this fee is paid every six months, it is not four percent deducted every month as reported in the Russian newspaper, but only one-sixth of four percent, which is 0.067 percent per month. This handling fee is a voluntary contract between the bureau and private individuals, and the service is exchanged for wages, so it is not a tax in nature. In particular, it cannot be confused with house tax, because its nature is completely different. This method has been implemented since 1932. This notice is hereby issued for public knowledge. Agent General: Piedian."

Yu Tang Horticultural School's Ephemeral Flower Blooms Suddenly, Wilts Within Hours, People's Education Center Has Filmed It

The Yu Tang Horticultural School in Shanghai County purchased an Epiphyllum oxypetalum plant from Jinling University in Nanjing two years ago. It grew ordinarily and showed no unusual signs, so it was treated casually. Unexpectedly, at the beginning of this month, this flower suddenly showed signs of budding, and bloomed suddenly at about 8 PM last night, with extraordinary cold beauty. The flower shape was similar to a lotus flower, white, and as big as a palm. A faint fragrance was revealed. Unfortunately, it only appeared briefly and withered two hours later. It is said that this flower blooms only once every three thousand years, so it is not easy to see. The Yu Tang People's Education Center specially set up lights at that time and filmed the flower, so that this ephemeral flower, which only appears briefly, can be permanently enjoyed.

Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Mutual Aid Society Opposes Tax Increase and the Process of its Establishment

After the rickshaw industry in this city established a mutual aid society to oppose the Public Works Department's increase in vehicle taxes, it has been approved for registration by the Municipal Party Department. The organization is complete, and the society's affairs are developing vigorously. Yesterday, the secretariat of the society issued a detailed statement opposing the Public Works Department's tax increase and the process of its establishment. This matter concerns the lives of laborers and unity against external forces, so excerpts are as follows:

Annual Meeting Passes Vehicle Tax Increase

On April 17th of this year, the annual meeting of Western taxpayers of the Public Concession's Public Works Department passed the department's various tax schedules, resolving to increase the taxes on rickshaws and handcarts. The original tax amount for rickshaws was 10 yuan and 5 jiao, which was increased to 15 yuan and 5 jiao. The original tax amount for handcarts was 2 yuan and 5 jiao, which was increased to 5 yuan. A public notice was published, stating that it would be implemented from July 1st. Therefore, the rickshaw and handcart industries, in a time when the city's economy is declining and all industries are withering, resented that the Public Works Department did not understand the difficulties of coolie life and suddenly announced an increase in vehicle taxes, which was extremely destructive to labor, and many expressed opposition.

Vehicle Owners' Meeting Resolves to Oppose

Compared to the rickshaw and handcart industries in this city, handcarts are three-quarters more numerous than rickshaws. There are approximately 13,000 handcarts and approximately 3,000 rickshaws. Therefore, the opposition to the tax increase was more intense in the handcart industry. After repeated consultations among the industry, representatives of the vehicle owners, Shen, Zou Shisong, Chen Shixiang, and dozens of others, initiated a convening of a city-wide handcart industry representative assembly to discuss methods of opposing the Public Works Department's tax increase. On July 7th at 2:00 PM, the city-wide vehicle owner representative assembly was convened at the Nantong Shanghai Fellow Association. More than 500 people attended. After discussion, the following methods were decided: (1) Organize the Shanghai Handcart Industry Mutual Aid Society to increase strength and unite against external forces; (2) Appoint representatives to petition the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Concession, requesting them to negotiate with the Public Works Department to stop the tax increase; (3) Autumn taxes will be paid after the negotiation is resolved; (4) If necessary, notify all handcart owners to bring their vehicles to the Public Works Department to petition. A vow will be made not to yield until the tax increase is revoked; (5) Issue a declaration.

Mutual Aid Society is Organized, Free Registration

Representatives Shen 1, Gao Youyu, Cheng Zhongdao, and one other person were appointed to deliver a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Concession to petition. The association accepted the petition and immediately appointed a responsible person to prepare the mutual aid society and begin soliciting free registration for handcarts. After the organization of the mutual aid society was announced, all industry members flocked to join. Those who registered were extremely enthusiastic. However, the Public Works Department, even after the Chinese Taxpayers Association forwarded the letter for negotiation, had not shown any indication of a response after a long period of time. Therefore, at the first preparatory meeting of the association on July 13th at 1:00 PM, it was resolved to send another letter to the Chinese Taxpayers Association, requesting a swift negotiation, and to appoint representatives to petition the Public Works Department and various Chinese directors and committee members, and to send letters to various organizations requesting that they uphold justice and provide assistance.

Yu Qiaqing Promises Assistance

On the morning of the 15th at 9:00 AM, representatives Cheng Zhongdao, Gao Youyu, Shen Yong, and seven others went to the Public Works Department and the offices of the Chinese directors and committee members to petition. Mr. He Dequi of the Public Works Department met them, while Mr. Yu Qiaqing personally received them from the Chinese directors. Both Mr. He and Mr. Yu promised to provide fair assistance. Mr. Yu Qiaqing also discussed with the representatives that old licenses could still be used before the negotiation was resolved and urged them not to panic and cause unfortunate incidents.

All Sectors Sympathize and are Willing to Provide Support Various organizations in this city, such as the Citizens' United Association, the Haimen Fellow Association, the Jiangbei Shanghai Business Federation, and the China National Products Manufacturers Association, have successively replied to the association, expressing sympathy and pledging to provide support. The Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Concession also continued to forward letters to the Public Works Department to petition on behalf of the association. At this time, the rickshaw industry also rose up to oppose the tax increase and sent representatives Chen Xiaoming, Feng Daowu, and Wang Wenyuan to the preparatory office of the association, requesting to join in order to jointly oppose the tax increase. After the third preparatory committee of the association discussed and agreed to allow them to join, the name was changed to "Shanghai Rickshaw and Handcart Mutual Aid Society." At the same time, the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Concession was requested to merge the cases and negotiate with the Public Works Department.

Police Detain Vehicles, Another Petition

Since the rickshaw and handcart industries jointly organized, the atmosphere of opposing the tax increase became increasingly acute, which attracted the attention of the Public Works Department. Therefore, detectives were sent to the preparatory office of the association every day to monitor the situation. The police stations even detained vehicles on the grounds that the vehicle owners were resisting the tax, and the number of detentions increased daily, causing the vehicle owners to feel uneasy in their business and creating an atmosphere of terror. Many went to the preparatory office of the association, requesting relief and protection. Therefore, on the 18th, Shen Yong, Cheng Zhongdao, Gao Youyu, and others were specially sent to lead the detained vehicle owners to the Chinese Taxpayers Association for another petition, requesting the Public Works Department to instruct the police stations to follow the instructions of Mr. He Dequi and Mr. Yu Qiaqing, allowing old licenses to be used before the negotiation was resolved and not to detain vehicles and deliberately make things difficult. Mr. Wang Xiaoxiang, chairman of the association, agreed to explain the detained vehicles to the Public Works Department on behalf of the association, and the vehicles were subsequently released by the police stations.

Opposition Results in Cancellation of Tax Increase

Since the association, during its preparatory period, had unswervingly and persistently appealed to all sectors for negotiation, the Public Works Department, at the meeting of the committee on July 19th, resolved to cancel the tax increase. This was submitted to the board meeting of the department on July 24th for adoption and approved, and a letter was sent to the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Concession to inform the association for reference. Therefore, the preparatory office of the association immediately notified all vehicle owners to pay the autumn vehicle tax as usual. At this point, the opposition to the tax increase was understood by the Public Works Department, achieving a satisfactory result.

Mutual Aid Society is Officially Established

Since the association was initiated and prepared, the number of industry members who applied to register as members, in less than half a month, already accounted for one-third of the city's vehicle owners. Therefore, on July 25th at 2:00 PM, a membership meeting was held at the New World on Xizang Road in the Public Concession as a temporary venue. More than 5,000 industry members attended, passed the articles of association, elected directors and supervisors, and officially announced the establishment of the society. Considering the rushed preparatory period and the tense work to oppose the Public Works Department, the licensing procedures were not completed with the Party and government agencies. Therefore, reports were submitted to the Municipal Party Department after the establishment, and the Municipal Party Department has approved the record. Looking at the success of this association in opposing the Public Works Department's tax increase, although it is said that it was due to the tireless assistance of the Chinese Taxpayers Association and various Chinese directors and committee members, it would not have been possible without the sincere unity of the industry members. Although the Public Works Department's license tax increase has been cancelled, it is difficult to guarantee that no other incidents will occur among our industry members in the future. If our rickshaw and handcart industry, with 15,000 to 16,000 households, does not have a group organization on weekdays, the industry's dispersion and lack of communication are self-evident. To be alert to the past, encourage the future, and seek improvement in the industry's living conditions and business development, the association is necessary.

Zhou Zujian, Weary of Life Due to Marriage Issues, Secretly Takes Tranquilizer Pills

Zhou Zujian, a 21-year-old staff member of the Hua Guo Glass Factory at 462 Xibao Xing Road, Zhabei, from Ningbo, was unhappy because his arranged marriage, based on his parents' orders and the matchmaker's words, did not conform to current trends. He suddenly harbored thoughts of ending his life. Yesterday morning, he secretly took three bottles of tranquilizer pills. By 1:00 PM, Zhou had lost consciousness. He was discovered and rushed to Doujiang Hospital for treatment in a streetcar. It is said that he took too many pills and his life is in danger.

Accomplices in Yangshupu Road Robbery Case Detained Awaiting Sentencing

On November 30, 1933, at around 1:00 AM, Fan Shengyuan, a rent collector in Changanli, Yangshupu Road, was robbed of 389 yuan in rent money. The robbers fled in different directions. Subsequently, the police arrested the suspects Zhang Xiaodeyu, Chen Lewen, and three others, and transferred them to the First Special District Court. After interrogation, they were sentenced to imprisonment and confessed that an accomplice, Duan Rujun from Jiangbei, was at large. On the 30th of last month, Li Hongsheng, a Chinese detective from the Yulin Road police station, received a report from an informant that Duan Dao (nicknamed "Little Pockmark") was wandering around Taihe Street, Yangshupu Road. He immediately went and arrested him and transferred him to the First Special Court for investigation. Yesterday, Judge Jiang Shuzi opened the Third Criminal Court for trial. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated that during the investigation, it was found that the defendant, on the afternoon of the 15th of the same month and year at 7:00 PM, colluded with a gang, held weapons, and robbed Xu Ronglan of the Zhonghua Iron Factory on Huasheng Road of 160 yuan worth of property in another case. He asked for a severe punishment according to the law. Subsequently, the victim testified about the robbery process. When questioned, the defendant confessed that he was invited by someone with a certain surname and did not enter the factory but acted as a lookout outside with a gun. He only received a few yuan afterwards and asked for leniency. Judge Jiang instructed that he be remanded in custody and await a scheduled sentence.

Tao Shuzhen Sues Wu Weixin for Assault

Tao Shuzhen, a former female detective of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Wu Weixin, who lives in Zhuangjia Lane, Menghua Street, were originally relatives. After Tao resigned, her finances were quite tight. Last month, Tao went to Wu's house to borrow money. For some reason, she had an argument with Wu and they grappled with each other until they reached the Wenmiao Road police station. As a result, the chief ordered Wu to lend Tao Shuzhen ten yuan and dismissed them. Tao Shuzhen then accused Wu of assault and other matters, and the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office, led by Prosecutor Zhao Chuanjia, summoned the case. After verification, the defendant Wu Weixin was ordered to post a 100-yuan bond and await further instructions. A public prosecution was filed according to the law. The day before yesterday, Judge Chen Kangsun opened the court for trial. The plaintiff Tao Shuzhen appeared in court with her private prosecution attorney Shen Xingxia, requesting a private prosecution. The defendant Wu Weixin did not appear but commissioned attorney Bao Gang to appear in court to defend him. The plaintiff recounted the assault and stated that the injury to her right knee had not yet healed. She requested that the law be enforced. The defendant's lawyer stated that earlier in the police station, the defendant, feeling sorry for her at the time, lent her ten yuan. At that time, she did not mention any injuries and signed a written statement with her fingerprint. If there had been any injuries, the police station would not have easily let her go. It is clear that the defendant was being falsely accused. The defendant, who is somewhat educated and runs a respectable business, did not want to stoop to such a level but was unwilling to be falsely accused and submitted a defense, requesting that the case be dismissed. The judge stated that the case still needed to be investigated and adjourned the trial for another date.

Special Article

Shanghai City's First Literacy School Management Situation (3)

— Wu Tiecheng

3. Achievement Examination Situation Regarding the achievements and examination matters of the first session of students in the municipal literacy schools, it is divided into two items: regular and final. For regular, the literacy teacher observes the teaching situation and selects important questions and sentence-making items from the literacy textbook for the students to fill in. For the final achievement examination, the method and procedure are stipulated by this office. The main point is to use 200 of the most commonly used and not very simple characters in the textbook as the standard, and let the students try to recognize them. Those who do not recognize a total of less than 20 characters will pass. Those who do not recognize between 20 and 30 characters will be ordered to take supplementary lessons and retake the exam. Those who do not recognize more than 30 characters will fail. This period, the exam will be uniformly held in each literacy school on September 1st, during the original class time, divided into classes. One examiner will be assigned to each school, totaling 218 people, and will be assumed by the education bureau, social bureau, health bureau, land bureau, public works bureau, public security bureau, public utilities bureau, finance bureau, and other eight bureau staff assigned by the municipal government. The teachers of each literacy school must assist in supervising the exam on site. The final exam results have now been statistically calculated, divided into adult and children aspects, and the number of students enrolled in each district, the number of examinees, the passing score, the number of students in remedial classes, the number of failures, and the number of absentees, as well as the ratio per 100 people, are listed. A statistical table is attached below:

Shanghai City Municipal District Literacy School First Term Adult and Children Class Final Exam Results Statistical Table Note (1) Check the number of students enrolled in each district, totaling 48,703, remove the number of examinees 24,583, count Yingxi 4,120 people.

Note (2) The percentage of absentees out of the number of enrollees is 29%.

Shanghai City Municipal District Literacy School First Term Adult Class Final Exam Results Statistical Table

Note (1) Check the number of students enrolled in each district, totaling 34,593, remove the number of examinees 14,176 people, count absentees 10,417 people.

Note (2) The percentage of absentees among the number of enrollees is 30%.

Shanghai City Municipal District Literacy School First Term Children Class Final Exam Results Statistical Table

Remarks

(1) There were a total of 14,110 students enrolled in each district. After removing the 10,407 students who took the exam, there were 3,703 absentees. (2) The percentage of absentees from enrollment is 26%.

(3) Children's classes are taught for two hours each day, which is twice as long as the one hour of classes for adults each day, so running one children's class is the same as running two adult classes.

From the above statistical table, in terms of the mixed results of adults and children, the urban area is better than the rural area, and in terms of attendance, the rural area is more than the urban area.

Comparing the results of adults and children, adults are better than children, and in terms of attendance, children are more than adults. Sports News

Li Huitang's Courage Remains Undiminished; Hong Kong Football Team Shows Off Skills with Decisive 10-0 Victory Over Western Team Yesterday; Hong Kong Team's Strength is Solid, Performance is Impressive; 15,000 Spectators Watch with Great Enthusiasm

The Hong Kong football team, which is attending the National Games, is very strong and has a good chance of winning a championship in this year's Games. To practice their skills, they specially arranged a friendly match against the local Western team at the Shen Garden yesterday. Li Huitang, the captain of the Hong Kong team and the "King of Football," also played, after having been separated from the Shanghai people for five years. Upon hearing the news, those who admired him flocked to watch, and since noon, the roads were filled with people. Before the match even started, all four stands of the central garden were packed, with a sea of people. Later arrivals had no place to stand, and the number of people was estimated to be over 15,000, making it a rare spectacle in recent times. As a result of the match, the Hong Kong team did not expend much energy, but with a minor exhibition of their prowess, defeated the Western team with a huge score of 10-0. The first half ended 7-0. Li Huitang was as heroic as ever, scoring six goals alone. The 15,000 spectators were so impressed with his skills that they were completely convinced and shouted their satisfaction.

A Hundred Penalty Kicks Reveal the True King

How are Li Huitang's skills? This is what the general public is eager to know. Li is the soul of the entire team, leading the troops and commanding everything. Without Li, the situation might not have been the same. His dribbling skills are so wonderful that the opponent cannot figure them out, and cheers are endless. His calmness and composure in front of the goal are beyond the reach of ordinary people. Among the six goals, three were particularly ingenious. The first time, he circled around the front of the goal and entered, the goalkeeper lost sight of the left while guarding the right, and Li shot in with a curved trajectory. The second time in the second half, the goalkeeper rushed out, Li skillfully dodged and lightly lifted the ball. By the time the goalkeeper turned around to look, the ball had already entered the net, which was incredibly wonderful. His shooting is also excellent, and his power has not diminished, making a loud bang. No wonder after the game, there were still more than a thousand spectators following Li, considering it an honor to see him. After Li Huitang, the most impressive player was the left winger Zheng Jiliang, who was as light and agile as a flying swallow, a rare talent.

Each Person's Technique Has its Own Merits

In terms of individual technique, in addition to Li Huitang, who was as heroic as ever and scored six goals alone, other players such as Bao Jiaping remained calm in the face of danger and repeatedly saved difficult shots. The defender Tan Jiangbai (who is representing Guangdong in this National Games) was commendable for his bravery, and Liang Xianzhao was also flawless. Among the center backs, Li Guowei was considered the best. Huang Meishun and Liang Rongzhao were also steady and decisive. The forward "King of Football" Li Huitang, needless to say, Zheng Jiliang was brave and handsome, and Zhuo Jinshi and Li Zhaorong were promising young players with extraordinary attainments. However, Cao Guicheng's performance yesterday seemed to be relatively inferior. The Western team is still a strong team among the Western football teams in Shanghai. Yesterday, in the face of the confrontation, they were completely on the defensive. Although there were several counterattacks, they ultimately failed to achieve their wishes, and it was difficult for the ball to get close to the Hong Kong team's defense, opening a precedent for the Western team's crushing defeat in Shanghai. The magnitude of the score was beyond the team's expectations.

Two Goals in Three Minutes

As soon as the silver whistle blew, the Hong Kong team kicked off in the center line. The "King of Football" Li Huitang led the forwards and swarmed in. Li Zhaorong scored a goal, and then Zhuo Jinshi scored another one in the same way. The two goals were scored in just three minutes, which was truly amazing. Li Huitang took a free kick from 20 yards out, but failed to score. So he showed off his skills, revealing his true abilities, taking the ball alone and entering the area. As he approached the front of the goal, he somersaulted and shot into the ground. Admon, who was facing the "King of Football's" unique skills for the first time, had no way to resist and could only nod in admiration, watching the ball enter the net.

An Irresistible Force, Scoring Seven Goals in Total

Having conceded three goals in a row, the Western team desperately counterattacked, spending all their energy to finally break into the Hong Kong team's defensive area. Wuller kicked the ball, but it was blocked by goalkeeper Bao Gang. Huilu came again, and Jiaping moved his fists left and right, resolving the danger. The "King of Football" Li received a pass from Li Zhaorong, raised his iron leg, and scored another goal. This goal was clear and beautiful. Li Zhaorong came again, Li Huitang took the ball alone, broke through three barriers, and returned with a victory. Zheng Jiliang broke into the border area as if entering an uninhabited place, and Li Huitang benefited from the chaos, creating a score of 7-0 in the first half.

Too Big a Difference, the Battle Gradually Relaxes

As the second half began, the Hong Kong team, with victory in hand, and the Western team, realizing that their counterattacks were ineffective, were inevitably demoralized. Therefore, both sides were not as fiercely engaged as in the first half. After a while, Li Zhaorong received support from Huang Meishun and scored the eighth goal. Zhuo Jinshi made two wonderful shots, and Zheng Jiliang probed for treasure from across the mountain. Admon's business was booming, and he was busy welcoming and sending off, trying his best to support the team. Only then was he able to temporarily maintain a partial peace. Before long, the "King of Football" charged in with his sword, and was eventually let in. Admon rushed forward to intercept, but the "King of Football" avoided the attack, lightly kicked the ball, and calmly put the ball into the net.

The "King of Football's" Ingenious Skill: Shooting into an Empty Goal

The Western team was now desperately counterattacking, and the Hong Kong team was a little more polite, to the point where it caused goalkeeper Bao Gang to become busy, and the Hong Kong team's goal, which had been quiet for a long time, became lively again. Li Guowei saved the ball from danger, and Li Huitang immediately entered the Western team's defensive area. Admon was eager to save the ball, but Li lured him away, lightly leaving his defense, hoping to intercept Huitang's ball. Unexpectedly, Huitang came up with a plan, kicking the ball over Admon and shooting into the empty goal. The second half resulted in a score of 3-0.

The total result was 10-0, with the Hong Kong team winning. The lineups of both sides are listed below:

Hong Kong Team

Western Team

Admon, Tuina (out), Crawford (in), Molai, Helei, Gibson, Mann, Huo Gengsheng, Wule, Huilu, Jack, Oklei

However, Lin was unable to make it due to circumstances, so Guo Weideng led the team, arriving in Hong Kong on the 2nd of this month and transferring to the Canadian Empress, arriving in Shanghai at around 8:00 am yesterday. They immediately registered with the organizing committee. According to Guo, the purpose of the Philippines' participation in this National Games is not to win medals, but to learn from the strengths of other athletes and make up for their own shortcomings, so that the sports of overseas Chinese can improve in the future. The basketball team members are mostly athletes from various schools in the Philippines and have some reputation in the Philippines.

Java Tennis: Xu Chengji and Others Arrive in Shanghai

Weary from Travel, Luggage Just Unpacked; Lin Wangsu and Chen Qi'an Suffer Setbacks Yesterday; Wang Wenzheng Defeats Chen Qi'an with Ease; Lin Wangsu Defeated by Xu Weipei Due to Lack of Energy

The Malaysian Chinese tennis championship athletes Lin Wangsu, Chen Qi'an, Ruan Guoying, and Yang Longzhang, who are participating in this year's National Games, performed at the Shanghai Tennis Club yesterday. Starting at 2:00 PM, the performance was held at the Shanghai Club court on Kangti Road. The competitive interest was even stronger than the first day's performance. Lin Wangsu, the "Left Arm General," has been the Malaysian Chinese champion for many years, and Lin Baoyao and Qiu Feihai have both been defeated by him once. Chen Qi'an is a rising star. He won the Malaysian Chinese championship last year. This time he returned to the country to participate in the National Games, and he has a good chance of winning the championship. However, the two of them performed abnormally yesterday and were defeated one after another. This was because they were tired from the long journey and had just unpacked their luggage, and their energy had not yet recovered. There were four matches in total, and the competition was quite fierce. In particular, the singles match between Lin and Xu was even more exciting. From beginning to end, the situation was tense. However, there were not many spectators, only about a hundred people. This was due to the impact of the Hong Kong vs. Western team football match at Shen Garden. The results of the matches are listed below.

Wang Wenzheng Defeats Chen Qi'an

At 2:00 PM, the entire Malaysian Chinese team arrived and the competition began. Chen Qi'an, the defending singles champion of Malaya, has good skills, and both his forehand and backhand are commendable. However, his serve is weak, which gives Wang Wenzheng the opportunity to volley. The reason for his defeat is also attributed to this. Wang Wenzheng's baseline shots are long, heavy, and powerful, either deep into the two corners or straight along the line, making it impossible for the opponent to save the ball. At the beginning of the first set, the two sides were evenly matched, each winning two games. After that, Wang Wenzheng cheered up and completed four games in one go, winning with a score of 6-2. Starting from the second set, Wang continued to win, going straight in and winning three cities in a row. Then Chen Qi'an took back one game, Wang led with a score of 3-1. Then Wang added three more games, taking an absolute advantage with a score of 5-1. At this time, Wang thought he had secured the victory and dealt with the game casually. Unexpectedly, Chen Qi'an responded calmly, taking advantage of the situation and winning three games in a row, falling behind by only 4-5. In the next game, Chen served, hoping to succeed in one fell swoop and tie the score. However, Wang saw that the good opportunity could not be missed again, how could he let it go? So he rose up and resisted with all his might, and indeed won the game. The result was 6-4.

Ruan Yang Struggles to Defeat Xu Chen

After the singles match, it suddenly rained, so the match was temporarily suspended. At this time, Carlsen and Defu had not yet arrived, so Xu Runpei and Chen Zhiqiang temporarily served as substitutes, competing with the Malaysian Chinese athletes Ruan Guoying and Yang Longzhang. It was difficult to tell who was better, but Yang and Ruan were slightly better. The competition was still quite fierce. The victory or defeat of a ball required ten or more exchanges, and each game required several ties before a winner could be determined. Therefore, the two sets were fought fiercely and took two hours. In the first set, Xu Chen was very strong and won with a score of 6-3. In the second set, Ruan and Yang struggled hard, responded carefully, and took it back with a score of 6-4. In the third set, Xu Chen had a very good chance of winning, taking the lead with a score of 3-0. Later, Xu Chen was anxious and flustered, and made many wild shots and frequent suicides, so Ruan and Yang chased to a tie of 3-3. Although Xu Chen had exceeded again with a score of 4-3, the good times did not last long, Ruan and Yang won three games in a row, ending the third set with a score of 6-4.

Xu Weipei Skillfully Takes Wangsu

The long-awaited singles match between Lin Wangsu and Xu Weipei followed, Lin is the champion of Malaya and Xu is the champion of Hong Kong. It was expected that the battle between the two heroes would be tense. Wangsu held the racket with his left hand and swung it freely, but because he had not been in Shanghai for a long time, was tired from the journey, and was unfamiliar with the venue, his performance could not be satisfactory. Xiao Xu performed particularly well yesterday, his shots were fast and he was good at running, and his cut ball was even more skillful, often making Wangsu sigh in vain. At the beginning of the game, Xu Weipei won two games in a row, followed by 3-1, 4-2, 5-3, leading all the way. Seeing that the opportunity was critical, Lin Wangsu tried to cheer up, worked hard to catch up, and drew long shots from both corners, applying pressure. Sure enough, he did not live up to expectations and also won three games, surpassing with a score of 6-5. In the next game, Lin served, but because his shot was weak, Xu turned it into a tie. Then Xu added two more games, winning with a score of 8-6. Starting from the second set, Lin calmly responded to the first set of defeats, taking the lead with a score of 3-1. Xu also showed his colors, tying the score at 3-3. Lin also won Xu's serve game, taking the lead again with a score of 4-3. However, Lin seemed to be exhausted, running slowly, and unable to cope with Xu's cut ball, so Xu won three games in a row, taking the second set with a score of 6-4.

Card Double Defeats Qiu He

The finale was the doubles match between Karlsen and Defu against Qiu Feihai and He Jialiu. It was already past 5:00 when the game started. Card are both veterans, with bold strokes and clear shots. Although Qiu and He are also masters, they are old and weak, their physique is weak, and the weather is late, making it difficult to distinguish between black and white, making it even more difficult to cope. Fortunately, Carlsen was only performing and dealt with it perfunctorily, not exerting all his strength, otherwise Qiu and He would not have been able to withstand the attack. At the beginning of the first set, He failed to serve, and Card won in a row, creating a situation of 4-1. Qiu and He chased up two games, and Card returned the respect in the same way, ending with a score of 6-3. In the second set, Qiu and He tried their best to fight, once taking the lead with scores of 2-1, 3-2, and 4-3. Card tied the score at 4-4, and then each added one game to make it 5-5. At this time, the sky was dark, so the match was stopped.

National Games Hires Mei Lanfang to Perform; There Will Be Entertainment Every Night from the 11th to the 19th; Movie Stars Hu Die and Others Will Also Appear on Stage, Making Every Night Exciting

The 12th Standing Committee Meeting of the 6th National Games decided to organize an Entertainment Preparatory Committee and hired Li Dachao, Chen Xiangtao, Chu Minyi, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Jiang Xiangqing, Lu Shoulian, He Tingran, Zhou Jianyun, and Hong Yanbin as members. Li Dachao was elected as chairman. The National Games Organizing Committee sent letters of appointment. Yesterday at 7:00 PM, the Preparatory Committee convened a meeting of various committees on the 9th floor of the YMCA in Baxianqiao to discuss the overall direction of the entertainment. Those present included Hong Yanbin, Jiang Xiangqing, Wang Xiaolai (representing Jiang Junyi), Lu Shoulian, Chen Xiangtao (representing Yuan Zengyu), Chu Minyi (representing Tian Shucheng), Du Yuesheng (representing Hong Yanbin), Li Dachao, and Zhou Jianyun. Chairman Li Dachao recorded the meeting.

Athletes from various provinces and overseas Chinese are very enthusiastic to participate, with a total of 38 units. Those who are responsible for performing entertainment activities will do their duty. If expenses are required, they will be borne by each group. Please give your opinions. The entertainment is divided into Peking Opera, drama, film, song and dance music, and magic. (3) It is scheduled to hold the second meeting at the Municipal Government at 12:00 noon on the 9th of this month. (4) Hong Yanbin, Jiang Xiangqing, and Li Dachao are responsible for planning and arrangement. (5) Jiang Xiangqing and Li Dachao are responsible for liaising with the National Games Organizing Committee for admission.

It is said that the repertoire is very exciting and completely voluntary. Dr. Mei Lanfang is currently singing charity operas for disaster relief at the Great Golden Theater. He originally had no time and energy to help the National Games. However, Dr. Mei decided to take time out of his busy schedule to perform his masterpiece. His enthusiasm is admirable, and the enthusiastic support of Committee Member Du Yuesheng and others is even more admirable. As for the songs and dances of movie stars, all the first-class stars such as Hu Die, Xu Lai, and Wang Renmei will be on stage. The 2,700 athletes from 38 units at home and abroad are overjoyed when they hear the news. The organizing committee is deeply grateful.

The Use of Badges and Medals for the National Games; Each Venue Specifies a Color; Restricted to the Staff of Each Venue

(1) Badges and medals will be issued by the organizing committee to all staff judges, unit staff, and athletes for identification.

(2) Honorary presidents, honorary vice presidents, honorary consultants, presidents, vice presidents, organizing committee members, preparatory directors, deputy directors, competition committee members, judging committee members, secretaries-general, and deputy secretaries-general will wear dark red badges with gold tassels and the name of their position embroidered on them. Those who wear this kind of badge will also receive a special long-term ticket for a special seat on the podium of the sports field (i.e., the track and field venue) and can freely enter and exit the stands of other venues.

(3) The organizing committee's judges will wear badges of various colors without the name of their position on the strap. The colors of the badges for the judges of various championship competitions are as follows: (1) Track and Field Games/All-Around Sports/Race Walking Judges: Red; (2) Swimming and Diving Judges: Purple; (3) Soccer Judges: Cyan; (4) Basketball Judges: Blue; (5) Tennis Judges: Light Green; (6) Volleyball Judges: Light Blue; (7) Baseball and Softball Judges: Green; (8) Martial Arts and Weightlifting Judges: Yellow. Those who wear the above-mentioned badges of various colors can enter the judges' seats specially set up in the south of the podium of the sports field (i.e., track and field venue) to watch the competition. In the gymnasium, swimming pool, and baseball field, except for the judges of each competition, they must purchase tickets to enter the seat.

(4) Staff members of various groups and sections belonging to the Organizing Committee of the National Games, except for the chiefs of the referee section, the registration and allocation section, and the venue equipment section, and the assistants and assistant staff of the registration and allocation section and the venue equipment section, who have separate regulations, will wear staff badges. They must purchase tickets to enter the seat when watching various competitions.

(5) The staff members and assistant staff of the venue equipment and registration allocation sections will be issued badges of various colors according to the color of the judges' badges and will be assigned to serve at each competition venue or provide consultation to the various judges. Those who wear this badge can enter the designated competition venue, but they still need to purchase tickets to enter the seat when visiting other venues.

(6) The chiefs of the referee section, the registration and allocation section, and the venue equipment section are allowed to enter the competition venues of each section, but they still need to purchase tickets to enter the seat when visiting.

(7) Each unit's chief leader will be issued a chief leader badge by the organizing committee, which can enter the staff and athlete seats or judge seats of each unit on the sports field (i.e., the track and field venue), and can also freely go to the stands of other venues to watch.

(8) Each unit's instructors and administrators will be issued short-strap badges by the organizing committee according to the color of each championship, with the abbreviation of the event printed on the strap. Those who wear this badge can enter the staff and athlete seats of each unit on the sports field (i.e., the track and field venue) to watch the competition. In addition to the instructors and administrators who participate in the championship competition in other venues, they can enter the stands with their badges. Others must purchase tickets to enter the seat.

(9) The organizing committee will issue athlete badges to the athletes of each unit. There are colored straps for easy identification of the types of participation. Athletes wearing this badge can enter the staff and athlete seats of each unit on the sports field (i.e., the track and field venue) to watch. In other venues, except for the athletes who participate in each competition, they can enter the stands with their badges (based on color). Other athletes must purchase tickets to enter the seat.

(10) In each competition venue, except for the chief of the venue equipment section, the chief of the registration and allocation section, the chief of the referee section, the judges who report their duties, the athletes of the competition team, and those who are separately stipulated in Article 11, no badge or medal can be used to enter.

(11) In the ball game competition venue, the chief judge of the competition and the coach and administrator of the competition team can also enter the venue, but they must comply with the provisions of Articles 29 to 32 of the special competition contract.

(12) If there are any matters not covered in this method, the organizing committee may amend it at any time.

National Games Propaganda and Transportation; The Central News Agency Sets Up a Radio Station

At this National Games, in view of the lack of unity in past conference propaganda, the strength of the propaganda group has been strengthened to seek accuracy and speed in transmitting conference news. Regarding news, the organizing committee has fully authorized the Central News Agency to use the radio station of the agency to broadcast various news at any time and transmit it to various places at home and abroad. The agency also has several ultra-shortwave radios installed in various venues of the conference to broadcast the competition situation at any time. This city fully supplies various newspapers with hard and soft news. As for photos, Wang Kai Photo Studio and International News Agency are responsible for supplying them. The Central Film Studio is responsible for handling the films.

Installation of Telephones Inside and Outside the Venue Completed
