*Shen Bao* Pharmaceutical Weekly

Scientific Research on Chinese Materia Medica (Part 2)

— Notes by Nie Zhichen and Wang Mingding, Lecture by Dr. Zeng Guangfang

Three thousand years before the common era, Fangji Liu Xiang set out to study all the *bencao* (materia medica) in the world. He collected all the famous *bencao* books of the time and made considerable efforts to organize them, but unfortunately, he died before he could complete this work! Later, his son Liu Xin continued his efforts and finally succeeded.

(2) Alchemy and Elixir Making: These belong to the Taoist school. They also have an inseparable relationship with the origins of *bencao*.

(3) As mentioned above, there are many names of herbs in the *Classic of Mountains and Seas*, which are closely related to the origins of *bencao*. However, there are many questions about when this book was published or who wrote it, and it is impossible to verify the facts. The herbs recorded in it are divided into four methods of use. From this, we can know the prototype of the methods of use at that time. The classification and usage of herbs in the *Classic of Mountains and Seas* are recorded below:

(1) Effective when taken internally: 68 kinds in total. Divided into: 21 kinds of plants, 47 kinds of animals.

(2) Effective when worn or taken internally: 29 kinds in total. Divided into: 17 kinds of plants, 10 kinds of animals, 2 kinds of minerals.

(3) Those that bring good or bad omens when seen: 52 kinds in total. Only animals are included; no minerals or plants.

(4) Those with medicinal and other effects: 55 kinds in total. Divided into: 21 kinds of plants, 30 kinds of animals, 4 kinds of minerals.

Here, we examine the four types of effective products and their uses as discussed in the *Classic of Mountains and Seas*: There is no doubt that the first method of use makes the herbs effective; regarding the effects of the second method of use, it is probably because there was no perfume at that time, and when encountering unclean smells, it was necessary to wear these fragrant herbs to dispel the foul odors; the third type, which indicates good or bad omens when seen, is sufficient to reflect the superstitious color of ghosts, gods, medicine, and healing at that time; the fourth type cannot be commented on.

*Bencao* in the Tang and Song Dynasties

The culture of the Tang and Song dynasties occupies a glorious page in Chinese history, and the historical process of *bencao* also took that period as its main era.

In the fourth year of the Tang Dynasty's Xianqing era, Su Jing and Li Ji felt that the *Shennong Bencao Jing* compiled by Tao Hongjing had lost its relevance and needed to be reorganized, so they jointly published the *Tang Xinxiu Bencao* (Newly Revised *Bencao* of the Tang). It had a total of 53 volumes, recording a total of 814 kinds of *bencao*. Su Jing and Li Ji were both high-ranking officials at the time. If we think about it, officials in positions of authority in the autocratic era were able to pay attention to the medical problems of the people and make considerable efforts to address them. It can be said that this was a major turning point in the history of *bencao*, from a private undertaking to a government-run undertaking, setting an unprecedented new record, which is also the precursor of modern health administration. In the 27th year of the Tang Dynasty's Kaiyuan era, Chen Cangqi wrote the *Bencao Shiyi* (Supplement to the *Bencao*) to supplement its shortcomings.

In the early Song Dynasty: Liu Han and Ma Zhong wrote the *Kaibao Xin Xiangding Bencao* (Newly Revised and Detailed *Bencao* of the Kaibao Era), which had 20 volumes. The content and materials were much richer than the *bencao* books of the Tang and Song dynasties. The *Kaibao Chongding Bencao* (Revised and Redetermined *Bencao* of the Kaibao Era) and the *Jiayou Zhu Bencao* (Annotated *Bencao* of the Jiayou Era), written by Liu Han, Ma Zhong, Li Fang, Wang You, Hu Mengtang, Yu Xi, and Su Song, are three books that are also most closely related to *bencao*. In the 7th year of the Song Dynasty's Yuanyou era, Chen Zicheng, a famous doctor from Sichuan, felt dissatisfied with the various *bencao* books of the past and emphasized the *Guangbu Zhu Bencao* (Extensively Supplemented and Annotated *Bencao*), which had 23 volumes. It contained records of his own experiences using *bencao*. In the 2nd year of the Song Dynasty's Daguan era, there was a Tang Shenwei who was not interested in becoming an official but was extremely interested in studying *bencao*. He wrote the *Daguan Bencao*, which was published by the imperial court at that time. He also published the *Zhenghe Bencao* with Cao Xiaozhong in the 6th year of the Zhenghe era. Although the names of these two books are different, their contents are the same. In the same year, Kou Zongshi deleted the ineffective herbs from the *bencao* and only recorded the practical herbs, writing the *Bencao Yanyi* (Elaboration on the *Bencao*).

*Bencao* in the Ming and Qing Dynasties

In the early years of the Ming Dynasty's Hongwu era, it was a time of famine, and people were starving everywhere. Zhou Xianwang Chengqi collected various *bencao* with hunger-quenching functions and wrote the *Jiuhuang Bencao* (Herbal for Famine Relief), which was published. The content was based on the *bencao* books of the Tang and Song dynasties. It is admirable that the noble prince was able to be so considerate of the people's hardships. More than a hundred years later, Li Shizhen used the *bencao* books of the Tang and Song dynasties and the *Classic of Mountains and Seas* as a starting point, and the *Daguan Bencao* as a blueprint, to publish the *Bencao Gangmu* (Compendium of Materia Medica). It had a total of 52 volumes, recording a total of 1,871 kinds of herbs.

Although various reference books for the study of *bencao* were published in the Qing Dynasty, they were not very valuable. What can leave a mark in history is the *Bencao Tupu* (Illustrated *Bencao*) written by Wu Qijun. Wu collected *bencao* from various places and made illustrations of the various forms in which they grew according to the different geology and climates. It is truly admirable!

Common Knowledge Q&A on Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(70) Catarrhal Jaundice and Acute Yellow Atrophy of the Liver

(Question) What is catarrhal jaundice?

(Answer) This is also a type of jaundice that occurs epidemically or endemically. It is more common in men between the ages of 20 and 40.

(Question) What are the causes of its onset?

(Answer) The pathogenic bacteria are unknown; most are caused by gastritis resulting from overeating and drinking.

(Question) What are the symptoms of catarrhal jaundice?

(Answer) Usually, general symptoms such as fatigue and headache occur first. Then gastrointestinal catarrhal symptoms such as abdominal distension, loss of appetite, tongue coating, nausea, and vomiting occur. The liver is enlarged. After one or two days, the skin and mucous membranes turn yellow, and the jaundice reaches its peak in five or six days. High fever.

(Question) What are the patient's bowel movements and urination like?

(Answer) Constipation, or occasional diarrhea. The stool is pale white due to a lack of bile pigment. The urine contains bile pigment.

(Question) How many days does this disease last?

(Answer) About three or four weeks; mild cases only last about ten days.

(Question) What is the treatment for catarrhal jaundice?

(Answer) Treat it according to the treatment for jaundice.

(Question) What is acute yellow atrophy of the liver?

(Answer) This is an atrophy caused by the lipid degeneration and destruction of the liver parenchyma. It is originally due to syphilis, a malignant infectious disease, or often affects pregnant women between the ages of 30 and 40.

(Question) What are the symptoms of malignant yellow atrophy of the liver?

(Answer) The symptoms of malignant yellow atrophy of the liver can be divided into two stages.

(Question) What are the symptoms of the first stage?

(Answer) In the first stage, gastrointestinal symptoms such as loss of appetite, nausea, vomiting, stomach pain, and pain in the liver area occur, and jaundice then occurs. This stage lasts about several days to two weeks.

(Question) What are the symptoms of the second stage?

(Answer) In the second stage, severe neurological symptoms such as severe headaches, restlessness, insomnia, delirium, spasms, drowsiness, and coma occur. At the same time, the liver shrinks, becoming half or a quarter of its normal size after a few days. Severe jaundice develops, and the skin, gastrointestinal tract, and uterine mucosa are prone to bleeding. Body temperature rises; it can rise to 40 degrees Celsius when the patient is dying. The pulse is rapid.

(Question) What are the patient's bowel movements and urination like?

(Answer) Constipation, with clay-like stools. The urine contains bile pigment and a small amount of protein.

(Question) What is the method for diagnosing this disease?

(Answer) Early diagnosis is very difficult; it should be distinguished from catarrhal jaundice, acute phosphorus poisoning, and hemorrhagic jaundice (Weil's disease).

(Question) Is acute yellow atrophy of the liver dangerous?

(Answer) Very dangerous. Most people die within two or three weeks of onset.

(Question) How is it treated?

(Answer) Only by injecting insulin, glucose, or salvarsan, etc.

Common Sense on Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Hygiene

— Tang Renjin

(66) Parotitis

Parotitis is also known as mumps. In colloquial terms, it is called "fried cheeks swelling." This disease often becomes an epidemic for a time. Or it spreads to a part of the region and becomes an endemic pain. It is most prevalent in spring and autumn. It is rare in winter and summer. It has the ability to transmit directly through contact. Therefore, it is often the case that the whole family can develop the disease one after another. Children and adolescents are most likely to be infected. Infants and the elderly seem to have immunity. Therefore, it is not common. As for the relationship between sexes, it is more common in males than females. Its pathogenic bacteria are not yet clear. Its incubation period is also not fixed. The average is about two weeks. The onset of the disease often comes with the general symptoms of mild fever. That is, a moderate fever, fatigue, dizziness, headache, and mild stomatitis. After one or two days. Parotid glands on one side. Thus, swelling occurs. Gradually rising. The earlobe is also lifted. The patient feels pain and tension in the chewing muscle area. So when opening the mouth, talking, or chewing. Most complain of difficulty and pain. If you try to press the glands with your fingers. Then feel soft. Sometimes it is edematous. The surface of the skin. Appears pale white. Usually after another one or two days. The parotid gland on the other side. Also has inflammatory swelling. At this time, both cheeks are swollen. The face is strange. Therefore, it is colloquially known as "fried cheeks swelling." If this disease has no complications. Then it can be completely cured in seven to ten days. The most common complication. When椎畢丸炎 (transliteration that I cannot find an adequate translation for). At this time, the testicles are quite swollen and painful. In women, mastitis, oophoritis, or vaginitis may occur.

This disease rarely has the risk of suppuration. If there is, it is due to secondary infection. At this time, the swollen skin. It becomes red and shiny. When you press it with your hand. Then there is a burning sensation. Its hardness. It is like soft mud. Submandibular and sublingual glands. Most also have swelling.

In addition, so-called secondary parotitis. Often occurs in several severe illnesses. Especially when suffering from typhoid fever. This is because the mouth is unclean. The virus invades from the parotid gland. Or it is induced by blood flow and viruses. The degree of swelling of this type of parotitis. It is very severe. And mostly forms abscesses.

The treatment for this disease. Is very simple. During the period of fever. Be sure to rest in bed. Apply cold compresses or ice compresses to the parotid area. Apply petroleum jelly or olive oil. In order to reduce the tension of the skin layer.) In our country, it is common to apply well-bottom mud to the local area, saying that it is effective. In fact, it is nothing more than taking its coolness to relieve skin tension.) The mouth should always be kept clean. When the inflammation is severe. Then apply ichthammol ointment. Or use a Solux lamp to irradiate. If orchitis occurs. Then use a提畢帶 (transliteration that I cannot find an adequate translation for) to raise the testicles high. Apply cold compresses or ice compresses to the scrotal area. As for secondary parotitis when an abscess has already formed. Then cut open and drain the pus.

Q&A on Common Knowledge About Teeth (4)

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 18) When do baby teeth fall out?

(Answer) Baby teeth must wait until the child is six years old, when the first permanent molar comes out, before they gradually begin to fall out. This first permanent molar can be regarded as the vanguard of the permanent teeth. When it comes out, the rest of the permanent teeth will also appear in turn to replace the baby teeth. This period of replacement is commonly called the teething period.

(Question 19) How long does the teething period last? What is the order of replacement during this period?

(Answer) After the first permanent molar comes out at the age of six, the above-mentioned five types of baby teeth will be replaced approximately one type per year. The central incisors are replaced around the age of seven. The lateral incisors are replaced around the age of eight. The deciduous premolars are replaced around the age of nine. The deciduous molars are replaced around the age of ten. The canines are replaced at the age of eleven or twelve (but the lower canines come earlier by one or two years). However, this is very approximate: the teething period varies greatly from person to person and from tooth to tooth; some differ by as much as two or three years (the above is calculated according to actual age).

(Question 20) What changes occur when baby teeth are about to be replaced?

(Answer) When a certain baby tooth is about to be replaced, because the permanent tooth grows and pushes from underneath, its root will gradually absorb and shorten, almost to nothing. Therefore, it becomes very loose. This is a natural indication that it should fall out. It is very easy to remove it at this time; there is also less pain.

(Question 21) What happens if baby teeth are not removed when they are loose?

(Answer) If we neglect this natural indication when baby teeth become loose, or if we indulge our children's fear of pain and do not remove them, they will still regain their firmness after a few months. The permanent teeth underneath will be blocked and will have to slant to the side. As a result, the teeth will grow unevenly for life. Not only is it unsightly, but it is also difficult to brush all of them when brushing, and it is easy to hide dirt and bacteria, which is indeed a major cause of tooth decay.

Domestic Medicinal Plants (4)

— Zhou Mengbai Lin Hongzao

(6) Bitter Yi [Chrysanthemum lavandulaefolium Makino var typium, Makino]

"Plant Description": Wild in the mountains and fields, it is a perennial herb. The stem can reach one meter in height. The entire plant is densely covered with fine hairs. Leaves are alternate, petiolate, ovate-pinnately deeply lobed, with elliptical lobes and wavy margins. In summer, it blooms with head-shaped flowers at the tips of the branches, with yellow ray florets on the outside.

"Crude Drug": Bitter Yi [Flos chrysanthemi lavandrlaefelu] refers to the flowers that are collected and dried.

"Medicinal Use": Used in decoctions to treat carbuncles, furuncles, and scrofula.

Traditional Saying: Bitter, pungent, warm in nature, with slight toxicity. Treats carbuncles, furuncles, and scrofula. Decocted in wine and taken orally, with the residue applied topically.

(7) Ze Lan [Gynura japonica, Makino]

"Plant Description": Wild in the mountains and fields, it is a perennial herb. The stem can reach sixty millimeters in height, with purple coloration inside and out. The entire plant is densely covered with coarse hairs. Leaves are linear-lanceolate or pinnately lobed, with coarsely serrated margins and sharp tips. In autumn, it produces head-shaped flowers in corymbs, with purplish-red coloration. The achenes have glandular dots.

"Crude Drug": Ze Lan [Folrm Eupatoru] refers to the leaves that are collected and dried.

"Medicinal Use": Effective in treating various pre- and post-partum conditions. It is an essential medicine for gynecology. For post-partum edema, mix equal parts of Ze Lan and Fang Ji into a powder. Take 8 grams internally per dose. The leaves can also be rubbed and applied topically to swollen traumatic injuries.

Traditional Saying: Treats hundreds of pre- and post-partum illnesses, unblocks the nine orifices, benefits the joints, eliminates traumatic injuries, and resolves blood stasis. Treats nosebleeds, stops vomiting blood, treats headaches, eye pain, fatigue in women, and sallow complexion in men.

(8) San Qi [Gynura japonica, Makino]

"Plant Description": Cultivated in gardens, it is a perennial herb. The stem can reach about one meter in height. The stems and leaves are both purplish, soft, and flexible. The leaves are elliptical-pinnately deeply lobed, with lanceolate lobes and irregularly serrated margins. It produces terminal corymbs of tubular flowers that are dark yellow.

"Crude Drug": San Qi (San Qi) [Folium Gynurae] refers to the leaves that are collected.

"Medicinal Use": The leaves and roots are effective for hemostasis in traumatic injuries. The roots are applied to the affected area. It can also be taken internally for hematemesis and epistaxis. Dosage: 10 grams, prepared as a decoction.

(9) Shu Qu Cao [Gnophalium Multiceps Wall.]

"Plant Description": Grows naturally in the mountains and fields, it is a perennial herb. The stem can reach about thirty millimeters in height. The entire plant is densely covered with cottony hairs. Leaves are alternate, sessile, oblanceolate-linear, and obtuse. The stems and leaves are soft. In early summer, it produces clusters of small yellow head-shaped flowers at the tips of the branches.

"Crude Drug": Shu Qu Cao [Herb Gnaphalu] refers to the entire plant with flowers that are collected.

"Medicinal Use": Shu Qu Cao is a cough suppressant, used in decoctions.

(10) Mu Xiang [Saussurer Lappa, Clarke aucklandia Costus, Falk.]

"Plant Description": Wild in the Cashmere region of northern India, it is a perennial herb. The stem can reach two meters in height. The leaves are membranous. Basal leaves are petiolate, while stem leaves are sessile, broadly rounded, irregularly dentate, sharply pointed, and clasping at the base. It produces terminal head-shaped flowers with dark purple tubular corollas.

"Crude Drug": Mu Xiang (Tang Mu Xiang) [Radox costi] refers to the roots that are collected, generally cut into pieces about five centimeters long, and dried. This product is cylindrical, slightly curved, with a dark brownish-gray wrinkled outer surface, resembling wood. The cross-section often has gaps between the bark and the wood. The core of the wood is often decayed. It has a unique aromatic odor and a bitter, slightly acrid taste.

"Components": The roots contain 0.3-2.78% essential oil. The main components are Aplotaxen C17H28 (chain compound, X , B Costen C15H24, Costuslacton C15H22O2 Dihydrocostuslatcton C15H22O2, Costussanre C15H22O2 Costol C15 H24O and other small amounts of Camphen CroH16, Phellandren.

"Medicinal Use": Mu Xiang is an aromatic stomachic. It can be powdered or soaked in wine for internal use. Dosage: 8-10 grams per day. It is also used as an important incense ingredient and can be placed among fabrics to prevent insect damage.

A Brief Discussion of Pulmonary Tuberculosis (69)

— Hu Jiayan

Chapter 12: Treatment of Pulmonary Tuberculosis

What kind of climate is most suitable for patients with this disease? The most important condition is, of course, whether the air is clean or not! In addition, factors such as temperature, air pressure, humidity, sunlight, and wind are also related. Places with a lot of dust and smoke are the least suitable. The differences in temperature, air pressure, humidity, sunlight, and wind are absolutely different between mountains and seashores, and between summer and winter. Even the respective disease conditions of patients are different, so the suitability also varies greatly. But generally speaking, seashores are suitable in winter, mountains are suitable in summer, and dry and less humid plains are suitable from spring to early summer.

Regarding mountain convalescence, ordinary people are often too superstitious, as if the illness can be cured just by setting foot there. This is of course due to excessive one-sided propaganda. In fact, not every pulmonary tuberculosis patient is suitable for mountain convalescence, and sometimes it is more harmful than beneficial. Severe laryngeal tuberculosis, pulmonary emphysema, intestinal tuberculosis, and concurrent kidney, heart, diabetes, and other diseases are all contraindications. In addition, if the body temperature increases above 38.5 degrees Celsius, the pulse is frequent, more than 100 per minute, the lesion infiltration area is too large, breathing is difficult, the heart is weak, and the patient is excessively anemic and prone to melancholy, mountain convalescence is also very unsuitable. These phenomena are sometimes extremely complex, so the suitability for mountain convalescence must be determined after a thorough examination by a doctor.

Medical Treatment for Pain Relief (35)

— Li Xing

Opium

Opium comes from the poppy. Dry opium contains about 10% morphine. Codeine is also a component of opium. Heroin is a product of morphine. Papaverine and noscapine are also lesser narcotics found in opium. The effects of morphine have been described in detail above. Since morphine is the main component of opium, the effects of opium are the same as morphine. Opium has a faster constipating effect than morphine, so the greatest use of opium in medicine is to stop diarrhea. Note that the use of antidiarrheals should be appropriate, otherwise it will not help with diarrhea. Codeine has the mildest narcotic effect and is used to relieve coughs and pain.

The chemical formula of heroin is: C17 H17(C2H3 O2)2NO HCI H2O. It is the strongest of narcotics. Its ferocity is greater than floods and wild beasts. It is easy to become addicted to and difficult to quit. It is a sharp weapon for destroying a country and exterminating a race. People must never try it.

Narcotic Addiction

People who are forced by hunger and cold are prone to take risks. People who are forced by pain are prone to fall into the trap of narcotics. Many people are innocent. When they are in pain, they are persuaded by ignorant people to try opium, morphine, heroin, etc. They only think of temporary anesthesia and pain relief as a source of satisfaction and do not know the danger of the future. People with weak willpower are especially easily fooled. Regular use of narcotics for ten days can lead to addiction. If used continuously for 20 to 30 days, the addiction will become deeply rooted.

When in pain or sick, do not seek comfort from narcotics. It must be understood that narcotics only anesthetize and do not cure the disease. Pain is sometimes an emergency sign of disease that requires proper medical treatment to avoid danger to life. Narcotics should not be sought. Using narcotics to treat acute illnesses is like a person falling asleep on a raging fire line. Even if one is unaware of the danger, the danger is certainly greater. Therefore, the only good way to deal with pain and illness is to ask a qualified doctor to use proper medical methods to resolve it.

Quitting Smoking and Drugs

No matter how brave a person is, no matter what kind of hero he is, once he is addicted to narcotics, he becomes an absolutely docile slave to narcotics. Why is he said to be an absolutely docile slave? Because slaves can sometimes resist their masters, but slaves to narcotics are not. He serves his narcotic master wholeheartedly and sincerely throughout his life, daring not to slack off in the slightest, and daring not to resist at all. If a person is willing to be a slave, then so be it. If he does not want to be a slave, then he should make a great determination to declare war on narcotics. Self-improvement depends entirely on this spirit.

The greatest power of narcotics is nothing more than causing people to feel (1) discomfort, (2) nervous disorders, (3) depression and annoyance, (4) craving for narcotics, and (5) trembling and a great sense of impending death when they quit.

Quitting smoking and drugs using scientific medical methods can be said to be without danger. The first thing to do to quit drugs is to make a determination. Although there may be some discomfort during the short period of quitting, the final victory can definitely be achieved. Here is an example: a person who had a long-standing addiction and smoked a large amount of opium, had been addicted for nearly 30 years, and was extremely thin. He said that he wanted to quit his opium addiction and that he must use the direct quitting method, without using substitutes. He made up his mind, went through some suffering, and eventually quit his opium addiction. This is clear proof of the success of determination.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Deepening of the Shanghai Recession

— Meng Ruo

Under the shadow of the economic downturn, recently four major businesses in the city, including Tianji Pharmacy, Yuan Xinchang Silk Fabric Store, Liyong Company, and Fangquan Bathhouse, have announced liquidation due to declining business and inability to maintain operations. At the same time, it is heard that the real estate industry is also very depressed, with few transactions and a feeling of being ignored. This situation fully demonstrates that the future of Shanghai's industry and commerce hides a serious crisis.

Shanghai's prosperity was originally superficial. Although some people are shouting that Shanghai is about to become London or New York, Shanghai's exhaustion is only increasing day by day. The collapse of small and medium-sized businesses has gradually made the market uneasy. The successive closures of large companies and banks are enough to shake the entire economic situation. The above-mentioned four major businesses? Tianji Pharmacy has been open for 20 years, and Yuan Xinchang Silk Fabric Store has also been established for 15 years, but neither could avoid collapse. The difficulty in maintaining business is evident from this. As for the real estate industry, it has always occupied a superior position. From 1929 to 1931, it was the golden age. Good real estate was fiercely contested, and prices continued to rise. Since then, it has gradually declined, and it has become worse year after year. What was once worth 500,000 yuan is now only worth half. This is another startling illustration of Shanghai's recession.

Shanghai used to be prosperous. Why has it plummeted and fallen into a state of depression today? There are naturally many reasons, but to put it simply, it is the impact of the global economic panic. In addition, China is a semi-colonial country and is also subject to a major oppression, namely the exploitation of the great powers. The hundreds of millions of yuan in import surplus every year were already unbearable for us in normal times. In the autumn of social recession, is it possible to hope that the countryside will not go bankrupt and the cities will not collapse? The great floods in various provinces across the country this summer are even more likely to make Shanghai become increasingly decadent in the future.

Regarding the sharp drop in land prices and the sluggish turnover of the local real estate industry, the situation has become even worse since the United States raised silver prices and implemented a policy of buying silver. As a result, not only the real estate and financial industries are in distress, but the general economy is also suffering a great impact. In order to alleviate this adverse phenomenon, real estate developers once decided to issue 50 million yuan of real estate circulation coupons, and also planned to establish a real estate exchange, but it is said that it did not have the desired effect. Recently, organizations such as the Shanghai Banking Association, the Money Shop Association, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce have also jointly submitted a petition to the Executive Yuan to formulate separate regulations to encourage the circulation of real estate. In fact, the recent bleak decline in the real estate industry is closely related to other industries. Before the economic situation can be reversed, industry and commerce cannot develop, and the real estate industry cannot prosper alone. This principle is obvious. The rent reduction movement in the city was launched based on this understanding. Rent reduction can directly revive industry and commerce, and indirectly rescue the real estate industry. However, although the words are good, Shanghai's prosperity is probably not something that will happen in the near future.

School Opening

— Bai Xi

On the day of school opening, Le Sitong, the principal of ×× Private Elementary School, changed into a faded gray-blue spun silk gown. People would say, "Mr. Le has put on a new dress!" However, on his face, the paleness and worry seemed even deeper than yesterday and the day before.

At seven o'clock in the morning, not a single elementary school student had arrived. His wife asked him to drink porridge, but he frowned and said with a sad face, "Why haven't any children come yet?"

Like an old ox that constantly plows the fields, he ran from the back door to the front door, and then from the front door to the back door. Elementary school students finally came, but not many. "What to do? If there aren't many students this semester, the rent, the debts... Oh, God! What to do?..."

Like an ant on a hot pot, his whole body was burning up. When he heard an elementary school student say that a certain student was not coming to school, it was as if he had been hit by a bullet, right in his worried and nervous heart.

Finally, it was time for the opening ceremony. The bell rang, and sitting in a relatively large classroom were only a few elementary school students. Facing these elementary school students, this principal felt like a prisoner facing the muzzle of a gun that would kill him. He did not say, "Today is the first day of school,..." The first sentence he said was, "Why are so few children here?"

So he picked up the attendance list from last semester and began to call out the names, making a special mark on those who were not present today.

"Why isn't Wang Xiangsheng here? Does anyone know?" His voice was crying.

Immediately, an elementary school student stood up and said, "I met him a few days ago and asked him if he was coming to school. He said he wasn't, because his whole family was moving back to their hometown, leaving only his father in Shanghai to do business."

"Oh, then, does anyone know why Li Shangen isn't coming to school?"

"Li Fangen?" Another child stood up

Page 18

and said, "His father doesn't have a business, and he can't afford to send him to school!"

"Zhu Zhiming?"

"He's selling evening newspapers!"

"Wang Xianxian?"

"She's not coming! She's going to a literacy night school. It's free!"

After that, Principal Le made sure to ask about all the students who were not present, but he didn't remember what the answers he heard were. He only saw the insidious face of the accountant collecting the rent and the extremely angry faces of the debt collectors.

Unlike the opening of school in the past, after saying some words of encouragement to the students himself, he would ask a few teachers to do the same. Today, after asking about the reasons why the students were not coming to school, he began to say:

"Children! You must try your best to introduce your friends to come. I have prizes."

Then school was dismissed.

On this day, Principal Le didn't eat anything. He sat next to the abacus and used it all day. His eyes seemed to be turning red.

Autumn Musings

— Liang Qiyun

I'm sick.

Suffering from neurasthenia.

The doctor at the hospital in the health department said that it would take a long period of rest to recover. But, in reality, I cannot have the kind of pure happiness that noble people are used to: I can only treat the courtyard of my apartment as the garden of a sanatorium after work.

(Autumn, you know).

(The beautiful flowers have withered, and the leaves have fallen; the season has a lilac-like melancholy taste.)

In a semi-sick state, the days sing a flowing melody, like the "flower after flower" passing away. Moreover, a sick person cannot be compared with healthy people. Everything feels lazy, and much time is wasted in boring idleness. As the days go by, there is a bitter and astringent taste that often surges in my heart like a tide.

The high tide in the ocean occasionally opens up the spring flowers in the heart.

I once had such a ridiculous amusement. —— Absent-mindedly, leaning against the window sill of the building for most of the day. In a trance, I gently closed my eyes, and suddenly felt a burst of sourness in my heart. When I opened my eyes, for no reason, two teardrops had already formed. …

So, I understand that slight melancholy is the only motherly comfort for the sick.

Although autumn is very lovable, it is always unhealthy.

Healthy people will never find the melancholy autumn lovely.

Notes from an Autumn Window

Outside the window of my small building is a parasol tree. Whenever the slight autumn chill blends into the twilight of dusk, the parasol tree slumps down again, falling into a state of slumber.

It is too lonely. Lonely with its green shade full of trees, and lonely with its sparse leaves falling.

——Why doesn't it bloom!

Sometimes, in the quiet evenings, I would murmur, with a mournful heart that almost cried out.

Because of this, I often like to lean against the window sill, turning my eyes following the clouds in the pale sky. I like to have a sense of desolation, making me feel as if my body is suddenly sinking into a bottomless abyss.

(This habit is definitely not healthy, because I would never think of these things when I am not sick.)

So, I stare without any real power. At the same time, I also think of some past events, the old rose-red dreams, the fire-like scorching days, and the youthful exuberance that young people should have.

The past is chaotic. It's just like autumn coming quietly and quietly aging day by day.

Yes, autumn is deep.

Seasonal illnesses have also worsened.

Looking at the depressed old parasol tree outside the window, I ask questions in my heart that cannot be answered.

——When will I be able to relive the wild dreams of my childhood!

Burial at Sea

— Da

Old Wang in the steerage lay stiffly straight on the straw mat. His emaciated face was devoid of color, as terrifyingly yellow as if made of wax. His eyeballs kept rolling upwards, exposing his bony chest, which trembled slightly. His mouth was open, and he was breathing with great difficulty, showing a rapid state.

The steerage was filled with the unpleasant stench of sweaty acid, and the pungent smell of moldy goods. The humid and stuffy air made people's heads swell, dizzying them, and making them vomit bile.

"Go quickly and report to the ship's comprador. It looks like he's beyond saving!…" A person in the crowd surrounding Old Wang's body, watching him take his last breath, swayed his head and shouted, as if urging Old Wang's relatives by his side. "How pitiful!"

However, Old Wang had no relatives by his side. He was just a lonely person!

"I'll report it for him. Alas, dying on the ship is terrible!" Someone in the crowd responded and came out, dragging his legs up the iron ladder to the comprador's room on the deck.

Old Wang was a man of about fifty years old. His gray hair was already a bit bald. Looking at the black teeth in his mouth, one could tell that he was an old foreigner who had lived in foreign countries for a long time. According to the story from a passenger who came down from the same port with him, he knew a little bit about his background. He (Old Wang) left home at the age of twenty to find life in foreign countries. There was a wife and several sons in his "Tangshan" (China) home. The expenses of the family had to rely on his foreign money. At first, relying on his ox-like brute strength, he worked as a "loader" in Hengfeng Gallery (shop), laboriously earning more than ten yuan a month to send home. Moreover, he would always return to his "Tangshan" home about every three or four years. Although life was not necessarily very extravagant, it was quite comfortable and was envied by his fellow villagers. However, the years were passing by year by year, and at the same time, his strength was also declining year by year. In the past, he didn't feel tired at all carrying a package of two or three hundred catties on his shoulders. His colleagues often joked and praised him, "Old Wang, you are really strong!" Now, needless to say, he couldn't carry things weighing two or three hundred catties, even one or two hundred catties felt a bit too much. Therefore, this time he returned from "Tangshan" partly because he didn't have the strength and no one welcomed him anymore; partly also because the market has been sluggish in recent years and the market has been depressed everywhere. In order to reduce the daily expenses of the shop, most shops were trying to lay off employees. Therefore, Old Wang also lost his job.

After losing his job, the lack of livelihood for his wife in his hometown added a lot of suffering and sorrow to him. In addition, the accumulated injuries from excessive labor in the past erupted like a volcano all at once. So, he fell ill. After recovering from his illness, some old friends finally gathered some money and sent him back to "Tangshan". Two days after the ship left the shore, before crossing the "Qizhou Ocean" in the black water, his illness broke out again.

Old Wang's deeply sunken eyes had slowly closed, and his bony chest had also stopped jumping and was resting quietly. The onlookers took out a light yellow piece of paper to cover his waxy yellow face.

The ship's comprador walked down from the iron ladder, followed by two cooks with coal dust on their bodies. They walked up to Old Wang's corpse, pounding, and roared.

"What bad luck, if you wanted to die, you could have died on the "Mountain" (seamen call land "Mountain"), fool!"

Afterwards, the cooks rolled up Wang's corpse in a mat, added two heavy iron plates on top of the mat, tied it tightly with ropes, and carried it to the deck. At this time, the onlookers followed him like a funeral procession, and everyone's faces showed a sad look.

"Thump," the cooks threw Old Wang's body into the sea, and in an instant the corpse was swallowed by the waves.

Transition

— Hua

One of the Trivial Records of Returning Home

When I stepped off the ferry, it was about to depart. The cabin was crowded with over a dozen people and several empty carrying poles. Seeing me as a stranger, they respectfully made room for me to sit down.

My memory hasn't faded. As a child, I used to take ferries like this to the city or back home. I would row from the countryside to the city in the morning and row back in the afternoon. This time, the rower was an old boatman around forty years old. He was bare-chested, with a dry tobacco pipe in his mouth, leisurely sitting at the bow, smoking.

The boat started. He forcefully pushed with a pole, and the boat turned around, slowly leaving the shore and heading towards the middle of the river. The muddy river water rubbed against the hull, making a rustling sound. The people on the boat seemed to know each other well. One moment, these few started chatting, and the next moment, they were talking about things in the city with those others. Only I was alone. I quietly listened to the familiar local accent, and for some reason, I felt a bit melancholy.

The damp river wind blew from behind me, puffing up our clothes and caressing the passengers' hair. The woman sitting next to me said irritably:

"Annoying! This damn wind! If the water rises again this year, we're doomed!"

Then, the old man rowing the boat opened his mouth:

"Did you see them in the city? How did it go? Didn't you make the trip for nothing?"

"Oh, don't even talk about it. The hearts of the rich aren't made of flesh, they're made of pig hearts, dog hearts," she said vehemently, suddenly glancing at me. I quickly lowered my head, secretly laughing to myself that she had mistaken me for someone else.

"Think about it, during the war a few years ago, they ran to us overnight, calling us 'Elder,' 'Auntie,' so affectionately, just wishing they could be more amiable. And I never shortchanged them. Now that we're asking for help, we have to suffer their scorn, and she won't even look at you." She said, pointing with her finger and stamping her foot. Because she used so much force, even the boat rocked.

She was a middle-aged woman with a pair of thick arms. Her face had long been painted coffee-colored by the sun. Her upper garment was covered with patches. When she spoke, white foam gathered at the corners of her mouth. There was really nothing about her that distinguished her from a man. She even rolled up her trousers very high, just like the farmers in her hometown.

I saw the boatman with the sunken chest shake his head and sigh. The boat immediately fell silent. The river wind swept past our ears, whistling.

"So, you couldn't borrow any money, is that it?" the boatman asked.

"Money? Guess what she said: 'Business isn't as good as it used to be, I can't move it.' 'Can't move it?' What she wears on her head, what she wears on her hands, what she wears on her fingers, it's all shimmering gold, and she says she's poor? Do you believe it! I even said I'd pay her back when I sold the pig in October, but she just kept pushing it off, saying she didn't have the authority to decide. Isn't that infuriating? Three percent interest a month, did she lose out? One day when there's lightning, that bitch better watch out, lest heaven strike her dead!" She continued to mutter. The people in the boat seemed to be absorbed, and who wasn't worried? Everyone's heart sank after hearing this.

The boat rounded a bend, and the Mazu Temple Pagoda came into view, towering majestically. I hadn't seen this tall pagoda in ten years. Looking at its reflection, at the gentle ripples of the water kissing the embankment, I should have been warming up my childhood dreams, but my heart was just as heavy. I just sat there blankly, lost in thought.

"Third Uncle, I don't have the ferry fare right now, I'll give it to you next time," she said again, her voice a little lower, and wiped the sweat from her forehead with the corner of her shirt. I could definitely find clues about the changes in my hometown over the past ten years from her, but perhaps she was just one of the most honest people, I thought.

The sun was already setting. The tall pagoda dragged a long, thin shadow, lying on the vast river surface, trembling. I thought in another ten minutes, I would be stepping onto my hometown that I had been away from for ten years. The scenery of my hometown must still be the same. This pagoda, this water, hasn't changed at all. But what about the people, my family? Especially in times like these, especially with these honest farm women, who are so poor that they can't even afford the eight copper coins for the ferry fare, giving me this heads-up, how could my heart not be heavy?

Raincoat

— Guiying

The sky during the plum rain season is always like a woman suffering from hysteria, with unpredictable moods. Just when a sliver of golden sunlight shines on the steps, before you know it, she frowns and starts to rain down fine droplets.

"The plum rain season is sometimes sunny, sometimes cloudy," he muttered, and couldn't help but think of raincoats. He should say he had raincoats; one new raincoat had a deposit paid, but hadn't been taken from the clothing store, and one old raincoat had already passed the redemption period in the pawnshop. Thus, he hesitated on the steps, unwilling to go to an extremely important banquet.

Like a monkey locked in an iron cage, he paced from one end of the corridor to the other, watching the increasingly dense rain silk splash up from the sky and the cement, slowly dampening the stone steps in front of the steps like an ink painting. So he moved in a little, pacing under a row of long windows, but the raindrops still greedily invaded, and had already sprinkled on his toes here and there. His heart seemed to be hanging in mid-air. He forgot that there was no room for him to retreat in this small space. Suddenly, his back hit the glass window, making a loud, jarring sound, which woke him from his daze. The sky was pouring down rain like a volley of gunfire, and the tips of his shoes were already half wet.

The appointment was definitely not going to be kept, but he wondered how long this plum rain season would last. He actually had two raincoats. The thought of that old raincoat being swallowed up by the pawnshop because he didn't have the money to redeem it made him unwilling. It was when he first graduated from university and fortunately immediately landed a position at the bank that he bought that beautiful raincoat with his first month's salary. But after that new raincoat was bought, the sky hadn't rained once. The sun was very bright every day, smiling gleefully. Occasionally, there would be heavy rain in the middle of the night, as if the house was about to collapse, but the next morning, the golden sun would shine on his window. The cement of the courtyard showed clean squares, and the buildings across the street, washed by the overnight rain, seemed like castles, reflecting the neatly arranged tiles in the light. Of course, the dust that dazzled the eyes rose again in the street. That new raincoat had been piling up in his box for several months, and the first time it was used was to be sent to the pawnshop. Initially, it was for an emergency, and although it could only be pawned for one-third of its original price, he planned to redeem it as soon as he got some money. However, he never had any spare money, and after adding interest twice, it was still forfeited by the pawnshop. What was even more unfortunate was the arrival of a rainy season, like the current plum rain season, with silk droplets drifting every day, as if to pay back the lack of rain in the previous season, never stopping. So he hated the rain, cursing the sky whenever it rained, and resolving to get some money again to buy a raincoat at all costs, even if it meant going hungry for a few days. Finally, his resolve was realized. He ordered a raincoat at the cheapest Western clothing store, paid the deposit, and arranged to pick it up in a week. Within that week, he exerted the greatest willpower to preserve the remaining cash... That should be a miracle, he lost his job. Until now, that raincoat for which he had paid the deposit had probably already been priced and sold by the store. He remembered clearly that there was a prominent line on the order: "All custom-made clothing not claimed within two months will be priced and sold." He calculated that it had been exactly three months since he lost his job. He raised his head, and the sky was as gloomy as his face. The raindrops blurred the glass window, and he could barely see his own haggard face.

Song Introduction

The Jintian Uprising Song

No longer be cattle and horses, no longer shame our ancestors,

The fields are barren and difficult to defend, we must plan for survival ourselves.

Remove straw hats and put on helmets,

The army directly points to ancient Yanzhou.

Let us all drink a cup of yellow dragon wine together.

Comrades agree with each other, kindred spirits seek each other,

Everyone bears the heavy burden of a thousand pounds,

Swear to fight for freedom this morning.

Return my homeland, avenge my generations of hatred,

Advise you not to waste your youthful years,

Be a national hero and be immortal.

There is no worry behind, and don’t feel homesick,

The flowery world originally has everything,

Make a long march of thousands of miles,

Abandon your family and children, break the cauldrons and sink the boats,

Kill all the barbarians and stop,

Brothers, bravely advance and strive for the country together.

Green water is long, heroic spirit is strong,

Work hard together and move forward,

United as a city, don’t linger.

Seize the flag and chop the generals, kill the thieves and capture the leaders,

Throw the whip and cut off the big river,

I only hope that success will be achieved soon and the victory will be celebrated.

Opening Chapter "One-Eyed Dragon"

Mr. Qun says is a one-eyed dragon, similar to a flounder,

Most suitable for looking at Western scenes,

One glance is clear, eyesight fierce,

Doing carpentry is good at snapping ink lines,

More suitable for spying on the sky,

If there is a golden leopard in the pipe,

It is easy and like a line is connected,

It can also peep secrets through the door seams,

And it is convenient to watch kaleidoscopes closely,

His eyes open and close to distinguish yin and yang faces,

Caring for the west is difficult to pass east,

If he happens to be nearsighted,

He needs to wear anti-wind glasses,

Just pay half the price,

Take the bill to fill the glasses,

Of course, this can save money,

Most worried about red eyes again,

His mother-in-law should marry a snail eye,

Or also marry a half-dazed with eyes but no beads,

This is a broken dustpan matching a broken broom,

A perfect match in heaven, a joyous meeting,

This is just an opening song,

To make you all happy,

Better than calling a church home.

News

The "One Thousand Opening Chapters" book is published by Shanghai Nanshi Wanyu Wharf Street West Section Ancient Song History Society. The book's content is to compile and mix various old and new opening chapters and secret versions of various storytelling masters that are not easily available outside. The whole book is a thick volume, selling for only three cents. All bookstores and newsstands are selling it. If you state that you were introduced by this newspaper, you can write directly to the society to purchase it and also receive a small autographed photo album of various famous storytellers.

The Yisheng Concert, for the Shanghai amateur music group, is organized by comrades who love music and glory, such as Kong Zhijia, Zhang Jienan, and Zhu Jianbai. It has harmonica, singing, Western music and other groups. Since the establishment of the association, it has been invited by the traffic radio station to broadcast a special harmonica program on the station every Saturday afternoon at 6:00 p.m., which has achieved remarkable results and has been repeatedly praised by the general audience. It is heard that the society's singing and Western music have also been organized in turn, and the singing has also been broadcast for the first time on the Youlian radio station last Sunday. The result was good, and it was again invited by the Shanghai radio station to broadcast a singing program every Sunday afternoon from 3:00 to 4:00 p.m. At that time, I hope that all those who love singing will pay attention to listening. (Yisheng)

Movie

"Sea Burial" SKETCH

— Bai Yun

It rained yesterday, I couldn't work, I rested for a day, and my spirit was nourished, so today everyone is very excited, Tian Fang got up early to sing "Boatman's Song", and Miss Fang and Miss Liu also smiled.

Work began, everyone stripped off their backs, barefoot, carrying fishing nets, walked to the sea, Paulu in front, Xiao Chen in the middle, old Wei blindfolded tightly followed behind them, a slogan, everyone shouted broken voice like singing "net song" up. The miserable sound of "Pull! Pull!" really wanted to make people unbearable to hear

The ruthless sun scorched everyone's back skin, soybean-sized beads of sweat, constantly tearing the skin out, the giant rope scraped the shoulders, indistinguishable from blood is sweat, gravel clamshell stabbing the heart, meat made of people, Suí also frequently called pain it? They were able to endure this sacrifice of flesh and blood under the direction of Director Wang, sobbing and swallowing. They are all brave warriors after all.

During the break, Director Wang comforted everyone and said, "You sacrifice, but that's only this time to shoot 'Sea Burial' in your life, which is nothing. You have to know that those fishermen who fight for survival are sacrificing like this every day! Their blood and sweat are scattered by the tide, and their bodies are also buried I don't know where in the sea, I believe that this sacrifice you made for the sake of filming not only increased the "strength" of reality in terms of the play, but also more lessons in your own life experience, you know, you really know the pain of the fishermen from today!" Everyone seemed to accept Director Wang's comfort, and gradually a smile of victory appeared in the bitter smile, which is:

The scorching sun shines.

Big sweat flows out.

Sweat is like a tide.

Droplets gather into the sea.

Overture to "Little Aunt"

— Chaoguang

Little aunt is like an eighteen-year-old beloved daughter, just waiting for the inspiration of the spring wind key, "Little aunt" is like a wisp of evening wind skimming a naked shy girl.

Little aunt with lotus petals blooming like a lotus, little aunt with morning mist, water birds, new water chestnuts in autumn pond, little aunt with snake-like body and water-like passion, little aunt with graceful and beautiful changes!

"Little Aunt" is: Husband is frivolous, little aunt is as beautiful as jade, but see little aunt smile, that hear wife cry?

"Little Aunt" is a poem: is Li Bai's "Spring Thoughts", "Little Aunt" is a painting: is Qiu Ying's "Morning Makeup", "Little Aunt" is a novel: like Ye Lingfeng's "Red Angel", "Little Aunt" is a landscape: like Yandang Mountain's "Dragon Qiu Flying Waterfall".

As light as the lake wind, as powerful as the raging tide, as vast as a spring dream, as fragrant as fresh flowers!

Female color is the source of disaster, which can sink the land, love is the fire of trouble, which can spread to the original!

Watching "Little Aunt" is like hugging a beloved daughter under the moon, stealing kisses under the flowers, watching "Little Aunt" is like boating on a lake in the spring with beautiful women.

Lake Scenery of "Boat Girl"

Young director Shen Xiling's poetic enthusiasm has deeply infected us in his past works. In "Boat Girl", Mr. Shen gave us more poetic and artistic images.

Xu Lai, a boat lady by the West Lake, lives a peaceful and hard life with her old father in Yunshui Township. However, because her old father is old and weak, he is already a little incompetent in this boating career. Therefore, Gao Gufei, a young and loyal man who is a worker who takes a boat home after finishing work on the lake every day, always helps the old man with the boat after the boat is opened. This pair of young men and women slowly pass on their love for each other.

Gao Zhanfei is the only one who sees it, and he doesn't have a wife yet. He always cooks and mends clothes by himself after returning every day, but one day, he was a little late. When he returned home, the rice was cooked and the clothes were mended. He was strange. He thought there must be a ghost in his house. He guarded against it every day, secretly peeping outside his door. This time, he finally saw that there was no ghost, but. His beloved boat lady, from then on, their love history took a step forward.

However, the good times did not last long, and his beloved boat lady was finally deceived into the fire pit by the fake artist. He himself was finally involved in prison for the strike problem.

Three Modern Women in "Three Modern Men"

Lianhua has "Three Modern Women", and the performers of these three modern women are Chen Yanyan, Li Zhuozhuo, and the late generation of famous artists, Ms. Ruan Lingyu.

Lianhua has recently created "Three Modern Men", and the performers of these three modern men are the three treasures of Han Langan, Liu Jiqun, and Yin Xiucen. It can be seen how funny it is to perform "Three Modern Men" with these three slender, fat, and rich treasures.

Moreover, it is said that there is also a scene of "Three Modern Women" in "Three Modern Men". These three modern women are naturally not Chen Yanyan, not Li Zhuozhuo, and certainly not the late Ms. Ruan, who? It is Ms. Han Langan, Ms. Liu Jiqun, Ms. Yin Xiucen.
